"Fairy, what use is this box?"

"Of course it’s useless, if it were useful, why would Time Immortal bury it?"

"He just felt the box was fairly useless, destroying it would be a pity, so he placed it where no one could reach, and look, he set up many restrictions in that secret realm."

"So the Ancestor is..."

"I guess he was being bull-headed, not following the rules, forcibly entered the secret realm, broke the restrictions, and triggered some kind of fail-safe, getting sucked into the box."

"..."

Lu Yang looked bewildered. Hadn’t Eldest Senior Sister mentioned that Celestial Master Guiyuan had vanished more than eighty-thousand years ago, without leaving a trace? Was it true that relying on his ability, he barged into the secret realm and ended up confined?

...

"Who’s there!" Si Lei God Lord watched warily as the burly man walked out of the Immortal Gold Box.

Withstanding the Divine Thunder and only getting his hair tips singed, this man’s strength was definitely no small matter!

"You strike me and then ask who I am?" Celestial Master Guiyuan immediately flared up with anger.

He had been trapped by this damned box for over two hundred years, thinking that he had finally been freed, only to be struck by lightning the moment he took a step out. Fortunately, he was physically robust, or else if it had been anyone else, they would have been reduced to ashes!

"You are the Celestial Master Guiyuan from Seek Dao Sect!" Si Lei God Lord remembered. The appearance of the three Ancestors of Seek Dao Sect was no secret, and during the celebration ceremonies, statues of the three Ancestors were even brought out for worship.

He was also a Semi-Immortal, quite active during the Great Yu Late Period, and after the establishment of Great Xia, he was one of the founders of the Five Great Immortal Sects. His status was not below that of Si Lei God Lord’s own.

"What is your relationship with Time Immortal, and why were you confined in the box!"

"Enough with the nonsense, just stand still and take my punch!" Celestial Master Guiyuan didn’t care about Si Lei God Lord’s identity, nor the current situation.

His reasoning was simple: I was struck without warning and now stand still and take a punch from me. Let’s level the playing field first before talking about anything else.

Celestial Master Guiyuan, speaking thus, sprang forth like a Flood Dragon across the sky, throwing a punch at Si Lei God Lord. His fist seemed to burn, bursting forth with endless rosy light!

How could Si Lei God Lord honestly stand still and take a beating? From his palm burst endless grey-white thunderous light, and with a push of his palm, he shattered space, as quick as lightning.

Upon fist meeting palm, with a boom, the thunder was smashed to pieces, turning into a scorching blaze, amidst which Si Lei God Lord was knocked flying!

Si Lei God Lord was in shock; as soon as he touched Celestial Master Guiyuan’s fist, he knew he had underestimated his opponent. The man’s body was terrifyingly hard, not something he could confront head-on!

Even a Body Cultivator at the Pass Tribulation Peak shouldn’t possess such a physique. How did he achieve this? Was it the power of his Dao Fruit Outline?

"Fairy, what’s going on with Ancestor Guiyuan?" asked Lu Yang.

According to Si Chen God Lord’s account, the Great Qian Dynasty harnessed the Power of Faith to create four Dao Fruit Outlines corresponding to the Four Ancient Immortals.

Si Chen God Lord and Si Lei God Lord were two of them. Si Lei God Lord possessed the Tribulation Dao Fruit Outline and, apart from the Dao Fruit Outline, he was also a Pass Tribulation Peak cultivator.

How could such a person be sent flying by Ancestor Guiyuan’s punch?

What was Ancestor Guiyuan’s Dao Fruit Outline?

"If I had known I would meet Ancestor Guiyuan, I would have inquired about the Ancestor’s Dao Fruit Outline from Eldest Senior Sister." Lu Yang felt a tinge of regret.

"As it happens, I’ve heard our old ancestor mention Ancestor Guiyuan’s Dao Fruit Outline." Meng Jingzhou came over.

"What is it?"

"The Unity Dao Fruit Outline, with the ability to merge anything into one entity."

"That explains it." Fairy Eternity felt clarified after hearing Meng Jingzhou’s description.

"No wonder the lad’s physique is so peculiar. He has integrated his flesh with Immortal Gold, clearly a power of the Unity Dao Fruit Outline."

Having merged flesh and Immortal Gold into one, one could only imagine how terrifyingly strong Celestial Master Guiyuan’s body had become.

Lu Yang took a deep breath. No wonder Ancestor Guiyuan was so audacious; he truly had formidable abilities.

"You still dare to block!" Celestial Master Guiyuan was displeased. This one was most dishonorable; you strike me and can’t even say sorry, and when I punch you, you dare to block.

```

Doesn’t reason apply anymore?

In the eyes of Si Lei God Lord, Celestial Master Guiyuan had gone mad. "You’re attacking me, can’t I block it?"

The two engaged in battle once again.

Taking advantage of their battle, Supreme Elder Jin Wenzhang unlocked the Law of Heaven and Earth, reverted to his original form, and took the opportunity to slip away.

"Are you alright, Ancestor?" Sect Master Kong rushed forward to support the Supreme Elder, helping him back to the Scripture Pavilion. He had been struck by lightning in the sky for so long that now he could barely stand.

Under the guidance of Sect Master Kong, the disciples of the sect finished evacuating.

The Scripture Pavilion had a defensive array method and was the safest place in the sect.

Fang Jin, Lu Yang, and Meng Jingzhou were also very concerned about the Supreme Elder’s condition.

"I’m fine, just expended too much energy earlier, a little rest should do the job." Having said that, the Supreme Elder stuffed an elixir into his mouth.

After regaining his strength, the Supreme Elder reflected on how these events had occurred: "What exactly happened? How come all of a sudden there are two Semi-Immortals here, one of whom is Celestial Master Guiyuan? Our sect will have to be rebuilt."

Gazing upon the pockmarked, damaged sect, the Supreme Elder felt a heart-wrenching pain. As the protector of the sect, his inability to safeguard it was a grave dereliction of duty.

"Do not panic, Ancestor. Our sect has bought insurance in advance."

"Insurance? Who bought it?" The Supreme Elder was surprised but took this as good news.

"It was Xiao Jin’s foresight, he purchased the insurance in advance."

"Nicely done." Learning about the insurance, the Supreme Elder’s mood visibly improved. Turning to Fang Jin, he asked, "How did you think to buy insurance?"

In the two-some thousand years since their sect was established, they had never encountered such a disaster. Generally, buying insurance for the sect would be a pure loss.

"Hang on, isn’t the appearance of two Semi-Immortals fighting in our sect because of the Immortal Gold Box you brought back, young man?"

The Supreme Elder suddenly realized that both, Si Lei God Lord and Celestial Master Guiyuan, had become involved because of the Immortal Gold Box.

Fang Jin did not know what facial expression to make. He had bought insurance, and then he brought back the Immortal Gold Box to the sect, which led to the battle between the Semi-Immortals.

Somehow, this didn’t seem right?

"Explain where this box came from in detail?"

Fang Jin recounted truthfully that he set out with Lu Yang to resolve conflicts, inadvertently collected the ancient map, and found the Immortal Gold Box.

"So you’re saying finding the Immortal Gold Box was purely by chance?"

The Supreme Elder believed it was a coincidence. Aside from the fact that Fang Jin had no reason to conspire against the sect, simply finding the Immortal Gold Box was quite fortuitous.

Fang Jin looked lost in thought. Could it be that Dai Bufan mastered divination, saw through the letter sent to him that Fang Jin would bring bad luck, and thus suggested he buy insurance?

In the sky, Celestial Master Guiyuan was still battling Si Lei God Lord.

Knowing he couldn’t directly confront Celestial Master Guiyuan, Si Lei God Lord opened up distance between them.

"So you’ve got a tough body, have you? I’d like to see just how tough it can be!"

The thick five-colored divine thunder pierced through the heavens and earth, shattering the void as if giant stars were falling, tilting the sky and slanting the earth, causing tremors within ten thousand miles!

Crack—

A bolt of divine thunder struck the Scripture Pavilion, causing its defensive great formation to fracture, uncertain how much more it could withstand.

The Supreme Elder’s eyes twitched at the sight; had that thunder struck him, his chances of survival would be slim.

"You think it’s impressive just because you can summon thunder!" Celestial Master Guiyuan scoffed.

Just as the five-colored divine thunder descended, Celestial Master Guiyuan activated the Unity Dao Fruit Outline, merging the entire space within a hundred miles with the five-colored divine thunder completely!

This meant that the power of this bolt of five-colored divine thunder was evenly distributed across this hundred-mile space, reducing the thunder that struck Celestial Master Guiyuan to nearly nothing!

```

Celestial Master Guiyuan’s flesh had fused with Immortal Gold, making it indestructible. The dispersed Divine Thunders had no effect when they fell on him.

But these were Five-Colored Divine Thunders, and even after dispersal, their power remained extremely terrifying. Ordinary buildings couldn’t withstand such Divine Thunders; within a hundred miles, save for the Scripture Pavilion, all was reduced to scorched earth!

"Divine Thunder descends from the ninth heaven!"

"Boundless Thunder Cloud!"

"Dutian Divine Thunder!"

The Si Lei God Lord, refusing to believe in curses, released different forms of Thunder Tribulations. Their patterns varied, but each had astonishing power, beyond what those at the Transcendence Tribulation Stage could contend with.

Facing different Thunder Tribulations, Celestial Master Guiyuan still used the Outline of the Unity Dao Fruit to disperse them. No matter how powerful the tribulations were, it was futile, enraging the Si Lei God Lord to the point of grinding his teeth in fury.

Since direct attacks with Thunder Tribulations were ineffective, it was time to try a different method.

"Heavenly Thunder Embodiment!"

With a light shout from the Si Lei God Lord, his form transformed, and his flesh entirely turned into lightning.

The Si Lei God Lord, in his lightning form, moved with inconceivable speed. In an instant, he was in front of Celestial Master Guiyuan, who, without a second thought, threw a punch.

But that punch passed directly through the Si Lei God Lord, hitting nothing but air!

"Haha, I’d like to see how you’re going to hit me!"

The Si Lei God Lord laughed heartily. In this state, he feared no tangible attack. No matter how sturdy Celestial Master Guiyuan’s body was, if he couldn’t touch him, any move would be useless.

At this moment, he was like the Thunder Deity patrolling on behalf of heaven, with the life and death of all living beings in his grasp, controlling all calamities.

"The boy from Great Qian is quite clever, knowing to transform into lightning," Immortal Fairy Eternity laughed.

"The Yingtian Immortal has used this move a few times. It’s slippery and elusive, like an eel. He bragged to me when he figured out this move."

"How then shall this move be countered?" Lu Yang asked, watching as it seemed Ancestor Guiyuan was falling into a disadvantage.

"Blow it up a couple of times and it’ll behave."

"..."

Ancestor Guiyuan can’t use that method, can he?

The sophistication of the Heavenly Thunder Embodiment went beyond this. Lightning is tangible yet intangible, penetrating everywhere. The Si Lei God Lord circled around Celestial Master Guiyuan, attacking intermittently with lightning.

Even if Celestial Master Guiyuan were stronger, he couldn’t possibly defend against all angles and block all of these strikes.

The Outline of the Unity Dao Fruit also couldn’t merge the Si Lei God Lord, in his Heavenly Thunder Embodiment form, into the space. That was something only a true Dao Fruit could achieve.

"I patrol on behalf of heaven; how could you possibly defeat me? Hand over the Immortal Box quickly!" the Si Lei God Lord arrogantly said. In his state as lightning, he indeed had the right to say such words.

"Palm Thunder!" Celestial Master Guiyuan flipped his palm, and a golden thunder appeared in the center of his palm, causing the Si Lei God Lord to want to burst out laughing.

Was he actually planning to attack his own self, possessing the outline of the Tribulation Dao Fruit, with lightning?

However, Celestial Master Guiyuan made an unexpected change.

"Unity!"

The Palm Thunder merged with Celestial Master Guiyuan, and he too transformed into lightning!

"I don’t believe I can’t touch you, you damned thing!"

Celestial Master Guiyuan struck with a slap, and the enormous palm nearly fanned the Si Lei God Lord into unconsciousness.

Both now in the form of lightning, they could finally touch each other.

"Ignorant and laughable; do you not know that I can control lightning?"

Though the slap from Celestial Master Guiyuan came unexpectedly, the Si Lei God Lord quickly realized the advantage was still his.

If Celestial Master Guiyuan had become lightning, then he was now within his realm of control!

With a mere thought, he could manipulate Celestial Master Guiyuan’s body at will, making him do anything he wished, even suicide!

"Stop!"

With a single word, the Si Lei God Lord pinned Celestial Master Guiyuan in place, unable to lift even a finger.

Just when the Si Lei God Lord was about to make Celestial Master Guiyuan hand over the Immortal Gold Box, he heard Ancestor Guiyuan bellow.

"Unity!"

The Si Lei God Lord’s pupils dilated suddenly. He found his body moving uncontrollably, flying towards Celestial Master Guiyuan and colliding directly into him, merging into one, with only their heads yet to merge completely!

One body with two heads, it looked bizarre and terrifying.

In this way, if the Si Lei God Lord wanted to harm Celestial Master Guiyuan, he would be harming himself.

Si Lei God Lord had never seen such a situation before and didn’t know how to control the body; Celestial Master Guiyuan seized the opportunity to take control and punched Si Lei God Lord in the head, knocking out two teeth.

"I told you to run, now let’s see how you’ll run this time!" Celestial Master Guiyuan said viciously, not looking the least bit benevolent.

This could not go on, Si Lei God Lord’s mind raced, seeking a way to break the deadlock.

His Dao Fruit Outline was very integrated, so why didn’t he merge the two from the beginning—was there some flaw in this move?

"Unbind!"

Si Lei God Lord unbound the "Heavenly Thunder Embodiment," reverting to his physical form, and as he had predicted, it forcibly disengaged the Unification.

There was a flaw in Celestial Master Guiyuan’s ability to Unify with a person—if both were in physical forms, it required mutual agreement to Unify due to the rigidity of physical bodies, making the process restrictive.

If it wasn’t in physical form, but rather a form like the Heavenly Thunder Embodiment with a loose composition, then forced Unification was possible.

Seeing Si Lei God Lord revert to his original form, Celestial Master Guiyuan also stopped embodying lightning to act as a living target.

"You want the Thunder Tribulation to scatter across a hundred miles radius, well then, what if I attack you everywhere within a hundred miles radius!"

"Ruishui Catastrophe!"

Although the Si Lei God Lord’s divine title was "Si Lei," what he possessed was the Tribulation Dao Fruit Outline, controlling not just Thunder Tribulation, but Heavenly Tribulation.

Ruishui surged, flooding the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect. Seeing this, the Supreme Elder did not stay hiding in the Scripture Pavilion any longer and immediately dragged everyone out towards the outside of the sect.

Preoccupied with battling Celestial Master Guiyuan, Si Lei God Lord had no capacity to pay attention to others.

Facing the Ruishui, which could not lift a feather, Celestial Master Guiyuan merged with the earth, allowing the Ruishui to wash over him.

The ground bulged as a giant emerged with the blue sky overhead and mountains on its back, making the already towering figure of Celestial Master Guiyuan appear even more massive.

The Ruishui that engulfed the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect only reached up to Celestial Master Guiyuan’s knees.

Semi-Immortals in combat, a devastation of heaven and earth.

Even though Celestial Master Guiyuan had the advantage, Si Lei God Lord was no easy opponent. After thousands of exchanges and when both had nearly exhausted their strength, Si Lei God Lord finally realized he could not defeat Celestial Master Guiyuan and made a hasty escape.

"To think of running away without apologizing, what a lucky idea!" Celestial Master Guiyuan said, perking up with energy. How could this man not understand decorum? It was one thing to not acknowledge defeat after losing, but not even apologizing first!

"Are you insane? Isn’t it enough that I don’t want the box anymore?"

Driven to desperation, Si Lei God Lord once again transformed into lightning and quickly distanced himself from Celestial Master Guiyuan; Celestial Master Guiyuan couldn’t force a Unification if the distance was too great.

At that moment, Lu Yang noticed that in the path of the pursuit, Yun Mengmeng was hastily approaching.

Initially, Yun Mengmeng had heard that the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect was in a remote and hard-to-find location, worried she might not be able to find it, but upon nearing the area, she saw that the battleground was indeed the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect without a doubt, and headed straight there without hesitation.

Lu Yang quickly sent a telepathic message to Yun Mengmeng, "Sister Mengmeng, stop the person flying towards you!"

"No problem," Yun Mengmeng didn’t expect to be entrusted with an important task immediately upon arrival and was determined to give it her all.

Boom——

Yun Mengmeng self-detonated, something Si Lei God Lord had never seen before, blowing apart his lightning embodiment and seriously injuring his true form.

Celestial Master Guiyuan, exhilarated, shouted and rushed forward, "Fellow Daoist, well done! Help me catch this scoundrel!"

Yun Mengmeng was startled; why was another one flying towards her?

Boom——

Following the orders of the Second-in-command, Yun Mengmeng was to stop anyone who flew at her.

Celestial Master Guiyuan didn’t expect Yun Mengmeng to self-detonate a second time, and was caught off guard. Which side are you on, fellow Daoist?

He had just gone through a great battle and had little energy left, so how could he withstand another self-detonation?

"Fellow Daoist, you..."

Boom boom boom——

Seeing that Celestial Master Guiyuan still had energy, Yun Mengmeng continued to self-detonate, knocking Celestial Master Guiyuan unconscious.

Soon after, Yun Mengmeng was holding Celestial Master Guiyuan in one hand and Si Lei God Lord in the other, presenting them to Lu Yang for commendation.

"Second-in-command, just like you instructed, I’ve captured them all!"

"Hey, hey, hey, Sister Mengmeng, don’t just go saying things; I never asked you to do that." Seeing Yun Mengmeng running over with Celestial Master Guiyuan, Lu Yang instinctively denied any involvement.

"Ah? Did I grab the wrong person? Second-in-command, don’t you want this one?"

Lu Yang pointed at Celestial Master Guiyuan, and Yun Mengmeng made as if to throw Celestial Master Guiyuan aside, frightening Lu Yang so much that he hurriedly stopped her.

"Don’t throw, don’t throw, I want him."

"So, I didn’t grab the wrong one after all," Yun Mengmeng said delightedly, feeling that she had finally managed to be of some help to the Second-in-command and very accomplished.

"Junior Brother Lu, who is this?" Fang Jin cautiously inquired about Yun Mengmeng’s identity. He had seen everything—the predecessor had knocked out both Celestial Master Guiyuan and Si Lei God Lord.

Although two Half-Immortals had exhausted themselves greatly, knocking them out didn’t seem like something achievable even in the Transcendance Tribulation Stage.

"She’s my boss." Yun Mengmeng declared proudly, then paused, feeling that something was off.

Oh, I misspoke. Chief Housekeeper is the boss.

"Second-in-command is my old..."

"Fellow sect member, we’re fellow sect members," Lu Yang quickly interjected. Sister Mengmeng, you really do dare say anything.

"Fellow sect members?" Fang Jin looked puzzledly at Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng. Would fellow sect members call each other "Second-in-command"?

You all really aren’t from a bandit den?

Fang Jin didn’t dwell on this too much, capturing Si Lei, the main culprit, was better than anything else, no need to worry about Si Lei seeking revenge anymore.

Although their Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect was just the victim and supposedly had nothing to do with Si Lei, judging by Si Lei’s behavior, he might hold a grudge against their sect after failing to defeat Celestial Master Guiyuan.

"The Third Elder said you two can return to the sect, no need to do unpaid work at the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect anymore," Yun Mengmeng recalled the purpose of this trip; capturing two Half-Immortals was just a side task, the main goal was to call them back.

"Speaking of which, where is the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect? The Third Elder said the scenery of this sect is beautiful, with stunning views all year round."

Yun Mengmeng, resting her hand on her forehead and standing on tiptoe, looked around, unable to find a place that could be described as "beautiful scenery."

Lu Yang silently turned his head, looking toward the ruins of the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect’s sect ground, inundated by Ruishui River, with mountains collapsed and earth cracked, feeling that even if he and Old Meng wanted to volunteer here, there would be no chance.

Moreover, now that they had found Ancestor Guiyuan and captured Si Lei God Lord, with these two major tasks at hand, they needed to return to their own sect anyway.

"Sister Mengmeng, let’s go back."

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou reluctantly said their goodbyes to the Supreme Elder, Sect Master Kong, and Fang Jin.

"Senior Jin, Senior Kong, Senior Brother Fang, we take our leave."

Sect Master Kong watched Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou depart, feeling very guilty. The two had almost met with misfortune in their sect; if something had actually happened, he wouldn’t know how to face Third Zhang.

"Master, what should we do now?"

Sect Master Kong thought for a bit and said, "Let’s first console the sect members. Leave the sect ruins untouched for now; I’ll send someone to inform the Jingzhou Branch to come here and assess our losses."

"The sect hasn’t been maintained for a long time; it’s a good opportunity to renovate it."

Knowing that he wouldn’t have to pay out of his pocket and that insurance would cover it, Sect Master Kong felt much better, as if he was just shutting down for a few days for renovations.

"It’s just the books in the Scripture Pavilion that are a bit troublesome. After being soaked in Ruishui, I don’t know how many are still readable."

"That’s alright." The Supreme Elder said cheerfully, "Of the three of us, you read the least. Chap Fang and I have memorized all the books from the Scripture Pavilion, so even if some books are unreadable, it won’t matter."

...

At the Jingzhou Branch of the Land Money Trade Association.

Upon hearing his deputy’s report, the Branch Head’s mind went blank, immobile like a statue, and it took him a while to come back to his senses.

"You mean there was a battle involving Half-Immortals at the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect?!"

He shouted incredulously, scarcely daring to imagine the chain reactions this event would trigger. The Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect had numerous buildings and unique landscapes, and though its value was unknown, it certainly would be more expensive than Sword Tower!

Sword Tower only had one building!

The list of failed investments was about to get one longer.

"How could this be possible, how could the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect have such an incident, weren’t the risk assessments for the seven elders showing extremely low risk?"

"And those seven immortals, where are they!"

The branch president immediately pulled out a gleaming machete, ready to confront the seven elders, but the deputy quickly stopped him.

"President, you forgot, the headquarters mentioned that several of their seasoned assessors had retired, forcibly transferring all seven elders away."

Only then did the branch president remember that all seven elders had gone to the headquarters, and being a branch president, he quickly calmed down to analyze the situation.

Damn, the insurance was bought just half a month ago, and the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect had an incident?

Insurance fraud?

"Explain in detail, what exactly happened to the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect!"

The deputy reported the incident truthfully, and after listening, the branch president could not find any suspicious details; it all seemed like a mere coincidence.

One side was Heavenly Venerate Si Lei from Great Qian, and the other was Celestial Master Guiyuan, who had disappeared for eighty thousand years; the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect simply didn’t have the capability to find these legendary figures.

If they had such capabilities, they wouldn’t need to commit insurance fraud.

"Just an accident?"

"Forget it, let’s have someone assess the damages to the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect first."

A day later, the branch president held a Recording Orb, which recorded the dreadful conditions of the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect. Viewing it almost gave the branch president a heart attack.

It was utterly destroyed, not a trace left.

Thunder purification, Ruishui River cleansing, the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect couldn’t even find a single intact item!

"President, should we compensate?" the deputy asked quietly.

The branch president’s body trembled, and he squeezed out a word through clenched teeth, "Compensate—"

"Ah, wait, we have an accountability system, the Shu State Chamber of Commerce compensated the Sword Tower without pursuing accountability, because they couldn’t locate the parties involved in the conflict."

"This time is different, the responsibility lies with Heavenly Venerate Si Lei, a Great Qian Half-Immortal’s savings should be enough to cover the compensation, right?"

The deputy had to remind on the side, "President, it’s true that the Great Qian Half-Immortal possesses Spirit Stones, but don’t forget that the Laurel Fairy Palace has captured the Demon-Subduing God Lord and the Demon-Removing God Lord of Great Qian, and according to the intel they provided, their savings are all stored in the Fairy Palace."

"Regarding the location of the Fairy Palace, they’ve been placed under a restriction, they can’t speak about it, and soul searching is useless, no one knows where the Fairy Palace is."

"Heavenly Venerate Si Lei might be facing a similar situation."

The branch president’s stomach ballooned with rage several times, but he finally slumped down, although it wasn’t good news, everything the deputy said was correct.

The deputy was level-headed and always made the right judgments; it seemed his position was truly well-deserved.

"President, I have an idea about this incident."

"Let’s hear it."

"Last time the Sword Tower had an incident, Junior Brother Lu was there; this time the Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect had an incident, and Junior Brother Lu was also present. Do you think it’s possible that it’s related to Junior Brother Lu?"

The branch president looked at the deputy, his eyes expressing some surprise, as though saying how could you think of such a thing.

"Tom, now I must say a few words to you."

"Please do."

The meandering stream flowed through the bamboo forest, where River Spirit, utterly bored, blew bubbles, showing only half of its head.

It yawned and from the corner of its eye saw Lu Yang and his group fly past, spotting the person carried on Lu Yang’s shoulder, its mouth agape for quite a while.

It rubbed its eyes vigorously, but by the time it looked again, Lu Yang had already flown away.

"Did I see a ghost?"

In the innermost room of the Task Hall, the acting master, Dai Bufan, finished handling the last task report.

"All done~"

Dai Bufan stretched lazily, feeling content as his official duties were completed, marking the most relaxing time of his day after a hard day’s work.

He used a magic skill to wash the ink from his brush, twirling it between his fingers.

"I wonder how things are going at Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect, those two little rascals didn’t cause any trouble, did they?"

Recalling the recent issue of *Cultivation Monthly*, which praised more than ten cultivators from Great Xia for taking the initiative to restore the terrain, Dai Bufan knew it must have been Lu Yang’s doing.

However, he was pleased with this, as it was a good thing.

"Though there should be no major issue, Junior Brother Fang Jin also mentioned in his reply that he had bought insurance."

Dai Bufan pulled out Fang Jin’s reply, which contained only two words—bought it.

Even more concise than his own letter.

"Good that he bought it."

"Elder Brother Dai, are you there?" Lu Yang’s polite knock sounded from outside the door.

"Come in."

Lu Yang entered the room with a beaming smile, puzzling Dai Bufan, "Weren’t you and Junior Brother Meng at Mountain Moving and Sea Filling Sect for a two-month study? It’s not even a full month; how come you’re back already?"

"Elder Brother Dai, we have great news! Overwhelmed with excitement, Old Meng and I came to report the joyous news to you!" Lu Yang said excitedly, his eyes sparkling.

"What great news?" Dai Bufan toyed with his brush as he wondered about the good news brought by their trip.

"Old Meng, bring him in." Lu Yang called out to the doorway.

"Right away."

Soon, Meng Jingzhou entered the room, dragging a mat with a burly, unconscious man lying on it.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou said in unison to Dai Bufan, "Elder Brother Dai, we have found the third ancestor of the Seek Dao Sect for you!"

"Gui... Ancestor Guiyuan?!"

Seeing Celestial Master Guiyuan, who had been missing for eighty thousand years, appear alive before him, Dai Bufan was so shocked he flung his brush away and leaned back, crashing to the ground with his chair with a loud clang.

He scrambled over the table to check on Ancestor Guiyuan’s condition.

Alive, but unconscious.

Yun Mengmeng stood firm, "But this is the only move I know; other moves wouldn’t stop him."

After spending time together, Yun Mengmeng had grown smarter and was able to understand the implied meaning in Lu Yang’s words, equating stopping someone with blasting them.

Hearing this, Dai Bufan felt his blood rush to his head, his brain surged with blood, his steps became unsteady, his body swaying, Lu Yang rushed to support Dai Bufan without bothering to discuss the situation with Yun Mengmeng further.

"Elder Brother Dai, are you alright?"

This man was truly a formidable ancestor.

Celestial Master Guiyuan, who had been sleeping on a straw mat, stirred. He groaned a few times, opened his eyes, and locked gazes with the curious Yun Mengmeng scrutinizing him, startling him into jumping up defensively against Yun Mengmeng.

This place resembled the Dao Seeking Sect he remembered, but many details were different.

It was up to Lu Yang to explain, "Ancestor, you entered an Immortal Box crafted by the Time Immortal. In the box, a day passes for every year outside. You spent over two hundred years inside, while eighty thousand years have passed in the outside world."

Celestial Master Guiyuan was indeed conflicted, "I guess I’ll keep this box. It doesn’t seem very useful, but then again, it’s a rare artifact crafted by the Time Immortal. It’d be a pity to throw it away."

Lu Yang really wanted to say that it wouldn’t be a pity to discard it. If he thought the box was rare, he could introduce him to the even rarer Time Immortal.

The Restriction was troublesome though. I thought, ’My body is so sturdy, even if I trigger the Restriction, I won’t mind,’ so I just barged in."

Upon saying this, Celestial Master Guiyuan regretted it deeply and slapped his thigh: "If I had known this damned box was so unreasonable, consuming me as soon as I triggered the Restriction, I wouldn’t have barged in!"

"It sent me straight to eighty thousand years in the future, and as soon as I stepped out of the box, I was struck by lightning. The person who struck me didn’t even apologize. After a hard-won victory when I was about to catch up to him, I got bombed several more times!"

Celestial Master Guiyuan felt he was truly cursed.

Lu Yang hung his head, too guilty to meet Celestial Master Guiyuan’s eyes.

Am I in the future or have I returned to the past?

Celestial Master Guiyuan felt as if he hadn’t fully woken up.

Before being trapped in the box, he had been the Ancestor of the Seek Dao Sect, the oldest among them.

How had his seniority dropped after he came out of the box?

How had Daoist Xiantian appeared?

Initially, he had felt sad, thinking that there was no one he recognized in the Seek Dao Sect anymore, but lo and behold, the founder himself popped up, leaving no room for sadness.

"Daoist Xiantian faked his death. He just woke up not long ago and had to Start Over after Disbanding Cultivation to escape being pursued due to some special circumstances," Lu Yang explained, being the first to discover Daoist Xiantian.

Especially when mentioning it in front of an Ancestor.

Seeing Celestial Master Guiyuan again, River Spirit didn’t quite know how to feel.

If anyone in the Seek Dao Sect had the best relationship with River Spirit, it had to be the third Ancestor. He had opened his Spiritual Wisdom thanks to Daoist Xiantian’s help. Celestial Master Guiyuan had been active for twenty thousand years, and Vast Sea Daoist Lord for fifty thousand years, making their interaction times quite lengthy.

But lo and behold, the two who disappeared had popped up again, and now his sadness seemed unnecessary.

He always believed that strength and realm were not absolutely related, whether one was strong or weak was something known only after clashing in battle. He had challenged Jiang Pingan, who had already become immortal, with this belief ten thousand years ago.

Regardless of the outcome of the battle, the most important thing was to stick to one’s own principles.

Ten thousand years ago, he had also wanted to challenge Meng Junzi, who had also become immortal, but unfortunately, Meng Junzi had not accepted the fight.

Although at that time, Meng Junzi insisted that he had not become immortal, but was a Semi-Immortal, he had become disheartened after losing to Jiang Pingan and stopped fighting altogether.

Celestial Master Guiyuan didn’t believe Meng Junzi’s tale at all.

If your spirit is disheartened, shouldn’t you go out, pretend to be weak and challenge others to regain your confidence? What are you doing staying at home all day? Are you the type of person, Meng Junzi?

Meng Junzi must have become an immortal and was harboring some evil plan to trap others.

Have we actually captured the Ancestor Grandmaster? No, what am I thinking?

Chasing Moon True Person couldn’t leave Great Snow Mountain and couldn’t come.

As the one who revitalized the sect, is it so hard to be number one in the Seek Dao Sect?

Celestial Master Guiyuan stomped fiercely, causing the earth to crack. He merged with the land, transforming into a titan that called forth wind and rain!

As he and the earth became one, as long as he stood upon the land, an unending power would surge forth. This move had given the God Lord Si Lei considerable trouble!

Celestial Master Guiyuan reverted to his original size, lying on the ground, his eyes devoid of life.

He was strong, but not strong enough to prevail.

He recalled again those glorious days a hundred thousand years past when he fought valiantly through bloody battles, breaking through boundaries in the heat of combat to become a universally renowned master, laying the foundation for the establishment of the Five Great Immortal Sects thereafter.

In those days, he called upon friends, overcoming countless insurmountable foes, filled with youthful exuberance.

Chapter 1092: Chapter 1091 Nine Star Spirit Chef

As Yun Mengmeng had guessed, Lu Yang had been very busy during the following days.

As the saying goes, love what you do; since he was to participate in the Spirit Chef competition, merely having the connections to qualify was far from enough. He needed at least a basic understanding of Spirit Chefs.

One of the fundamental skills of a Spirit Chef, for example, is bone and meat removal without damaging the bones.

Spirit Chefs have their own ranking system, divided into nine stars, corresponding to the stages of Qi Cultivation, Foundation Establishment, Golden Core, Nascent Soul, Divinity Transformation, Void Refinement, Body Integration, Transcendance Tribulation, and Immortal.

The Qi Cultivation stage corresponds to one star, while the Immortal corresponds to nine stars.

A six-star Spirit Chef at the Void Refinement stage is basically just a title. When a five-star Spirit Chef from the Divinity Transformation stage advances to the Void Refinement Stage, the Spirit Chef Alliance grants them the title of six-star Spirit Chef.

There is only one nine-star Spirit Chef, and that is the legendary Ancestor of Spirit Chefs, Yingtian Immortal!

Lu Yang had uniquely favorable conditions for studying the Spirit Chef knowledge, as the real legendary nine-star Spirit Chef, Fairy Eternity, personally taught him.

"Little Yang, look, this is the structure of the Kui Ox. This white line is where the bone meets the meat. When removing bones and flesh, start at the seam."

In the Spiritual Space, Fairy Eternity squatted on the ground, drawing simplified sketches with a stick. If she hadn’t said this was a Kui Ox, Lu Yang might have thought it was a skewer of two hawthorns, the first one being the head and the second the body.

"Fairy, maybe we should get a real object to practice on," Lu Yang earnestly suggested. At this rate, he feared he would forget what a real Kui Ox looked like, let alone learn how to debone one.

However, Lu Yang couldn’t directly criticize Fairy Eternity’s drawing skills; changing a Spirit Chef to learn from might hurt her feelings.

"Getting a real object, that might indeed be a good idea."

What Lu Yang needed wasn’t just the body of a Kui Ox, but many bodies of Demon Beasts.

Lu Yang took a deep breath twice, discarded distracting thoughts, paid no attention to the activities on Song Tianjing’s side, and stopped thinking about his doom. What he needed to do now was to focus on displaying his knife skills.

Other stages he could just experience lightly, but the first stage required his full effort.

As they say, there’s no difference between knife and sword, often a Sword Cultivator’s use of a knife is not inferior either; he, with his Sword Spirit Root and renowned as the premier Sword Cultivator of his level, could not lose face in this challenge!

The Five Star Spirit Chef Team was also in the Beast Fighting Arena where Divine Transformation Stage Demon Beasts broke free from their cages, wantonly unleashing their oppressive might.

Merely the oppressive force was enough to scare away some Spirit Chefs, preventing them from acting and causing their hands holding the knives to tremble.

But Lu Yang was certainly not among them! freewebnovel.com

Other Five Star Spirit Chefs had their own unique equipment; Lu Yang was different, as a simple kitchen knife was enough for him.

The competition for the Five Star Spirit Chef Team was slightly different from that of the Two Star Spirit Chef Team, as there was an additional requirement in the topic.

"Vice Alliance Hierarch Liu Xing just said that in knife skills, ’benevolence’ must be reflected."

Lu Yang was still pondering what "Knife Skills" meant, while other Spirit Chefs had already formed their ideas and began slicing.

"Look quick, there’s a small sun!" The audience noticed something unusual about the Five Star Spirit Chef Team.

"No, no, that’s not a small sun, it’s Golden Blade Master, it’s his golden knife shaving so rapidly!"

Golden Blade Master took the lead, choosing a Fei Yi, which was a kind of snake from the Snake Clan, with six legs and four wings, ranking fifth among the Divine Transformation Demon Beasts!

Repeating his old trick, Golden Blade Master stomped his feet down, muscles bulging, suddenly throwing the Fei Yi into the sky.

"Bone Stripping Blade Technique!"

Two golden knives flew swiftly, resembling a great sun, leaving clean snake bones and falling white snake meat wherever the sunlight touched.

"The goodness in knife skills lies in not letting the Demon Beast feel pain, yielding matters," Golden Blade Master hung his golden knives in front of his chest and indifferently spoke, he landed first, followed by the white snake meat falling like rain into the plates.

In fact, Golden Blade Master also had the capability to defeat the first four ranked Demon Beasts; however, not being able to kill instantaneously, inducing pain in the Demon Beast, would not count as benevolent knife skills.

"Why is there such a dense mist over there?"

"Amidst the mist, there’s a figure dancing beautifully, is it a fairy dancing?" The audience became excited again.

After the mist dissipated, it turned out not to be a fairy but Poisonous Granny dissecting a poisoned Nine-headed Lion.

Yun Mengmeng looked at the audience with a strange gaze; did these people have something wrong with their eyes, seeing both a small sun and a fairy dancing?

During the competition, Poisonous Granny temporarily didn’t need to wear handcuffs and shackles, feeling much lighter.

She gave a sinister smile, choosing the Nine-headed Lion, which was one of the top three formidable beings.

Poisonous Granny let the Nine-headed Lion bite into her, tearing off a piece of flesh; poisonous blood flowed out, turning into a toxic mist upon contact with air, sending the Nine-headed Lion into a wonderful slumber.

"The goodness in knife skills is having the Demon Beast die in bliss!"

Apart from Lu Yang, there was one more person who did nothing from the beginning to the end, and that was Ma Bin.

"The goodness in knife skills, so that’s what it means."

Ma Bin raised his hand and summoned Vice Alliance Hierarch Liu Xing.

"Do you need something?"

"I forfeit."

"Yes, the essence of knife skills lies in not killing, only by forfeiting can I avoid killing!"

"Have you truly thought this through, is that your final answer?"

"Yes!" Ma Bin nodded.

"Alright, you may leave then."

"Have I passed the test?"

Liu Xing rolled his eyes, pointing at the spectator seats, "You’ve forfeited and still think you can pass the test, go sit in the spectator seats."

"..."

This wasn’t right, wouldn’t Vice Alliance Leader Liu reveal a meaningful smile, acknowledging that I had understood the purpose of the test and let me pass on my own?

How could my Imperial Kitchen’s knife fame end like this?

Ma Bin was sent to the spectator seats, but the competition continued.

Finally, Lu Yang made a move; he slowly stood up, holding an ordinary kitchen knife, and strolled towards the Beast King Kui Niu.

The Kui Niu, sensing danger, knew instinctively from its bloodline that this enemy could kill it!

Lu Yang raised his knife and then lowered it, while the Kui Niu stood still, completely unharmed.

"What happened, what’s going on?" The audience was extremely puzzled. Was he just intimidating the Kui Niu?

Is this the level of the Immortal Chef’s successor?

"No, look what he’s holding in his hand!" Ma Bin, possessing genuine skill, quickly noticed something unusual.

At some unknown point, Lu Yang held in his hand an extremely thin piece of paper, nearly transparent under the sunlight.

"Let me see." Liu Xing instantly moved closer, took the paper which felt weightless.

He unfolded it, and to his surprise, it was in the shape of the Kui Niu!

"You did this..."

"I split the Kui Niu down the middle, made another cut along the cross-section, and obtained this piece of beef paper."

"And the Kui Niu didn’t even realize it had been cut, the wounds healed immediately."

Lu Yang tore off a small piece of the beef paper and chewed it, the flavor of Kui Niu meat filling his mouth.

"I think Ma Bin is right, the essence of knife skills truly lies in not killing. Vice Alliance Hierarch, would you like to try?"

The beef paper was so thin that a bit of sunlight was enough to cook it!

"No, your knife skills are superb, but the beef paper is too thin, not even enough for one dish. Despite demonstrating the essence of knife skills, you are not a qualified Spirit Chef." Liu Xing was very strict in terms of Spirit Chef standards.

"Why would that be difficult?" Lu Yang chuckled, knocked the Kui Niu out with the back of his knife, raised his knife again, and then had a piece of meat with a marbled pattern in his hand!

Liu Xing’s pupils dilated, showing a disbelief expression.

Now he saw it clearly; to an untrained eye, it seemed like just one cut, but he saw Lu Yang make eighty-one cuts!

After knocking out the Kui Niu, Lu Yang made one cut to open its skin, extracted the beef shank, and after removing the beef shank, the Kui Niu’s skin had just healed!

The Kui Niu, a Divinity Transformation Stage Demon Beast, had extremely strong healing abilities. By the time it awoke, the missing part had already regrown!

And the Kui Niu had no idea!

"If Vice Alliance Hierarch still thinks it’s not enough food, I can find a few more Kui Nius. I can cut parts from them, and that should add up to a whole Kui Niu."

"You, you’ve passed." Vice Alliance Hierarch Liu said dazedly, this was more than just passing, it was a record-setting, an unprecedented knife technique in the sixty thousand year history of the Spirit Chef competition within the Five Star Spirit Chef Team!

"By the way, how many cuts did you make just now?" Vice Alliance Leader Liu suddenly asked before leaving.

Lu Yang smiled lightly, clasping his fists:

"A hundred and eight cuts, I am gratified."

This was the type of man their Taotie Clan should cultivate vigorously.

In other words, only five people would pass this round!

It’s such a bother. If only he had brought Old Meng along, then he could concentrate on having fun and let him fret over this problem.

Golden Blade Master sent a beam of Spiritual Energy into the sky, signaling his readiness to answer the question.

"Incorrect answer."

The first Spirit Chef was quickly eliminated, and it was none other than Golden Blade Master, who had performed so well in the knife skills challenge.

[Immortal Tongue]Xie Bin.

He was very familiar with this as the Seek Dao Sect’s herb garden hosted a Kirin Immortality Medicine that had originated from Ancient Times.

On the day of the Qilin Immortal’s grand wedding, Fairy Eternity accidentally interfered, leading to Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi competing in a culinary showdown, prompting the Yingtian Immortal to taste. The three immortals, unaware of the truth, blamed the Qilin Immortal for the chaos and gave him a beating. During that battle, a few drops of blood from the Qilin Immortal, which contained his life-creating powers, birthed the later generations’ Kirin Immortality Medicine.

[Immortal Tongue]Xie Qi, [Invincible]An Tong, [Poisonous Granny], and others had heard of the Immortal Elixir but only by name and were unaware of its origins.

Lu Yang, hands clasped behind his back, strolled around, then slowly began to relay an ancient secret tale.

The Qilin Immortal stood alone against three and did not falter. Too many Star Cores eaten?

Chapter 1099: Chapter 1098: Fish Not Fish

Who is Ao Ling? A Dragon Clan Ancestor, the strongest Semi-Immortal, second only in prestige within the Demon Race to the Qilin Immortal, far beyond what Zhu Tian could compare to.

Lu Yang was fortunate enough to awaken Ao Ling in the East Sea, earning the qualification to meet her. The Spirit Chef Alliance did not possess such capability.

Moreover, there was no need to have Ao Ling come to verify the authenticity, as Lu Yang’s reputation and identity were enough to explain everything.

If Lu Yang said it was an Immortal Fruit, then it was an Immortal Fruit.

"Lu Yang was actually a Spirit Chef as well?" The audience had yet to recover from the revelation of Lu Yang’s identity.

Poisonous Granny hung her head dejectedly; she had guessed this would be the outcome as soon as Lu Yang appeared.

Two officers from Great Xia came, shackling her wrists and ankles, and escorted her back to Great Xia to continue her sentence.

The two officers from Great Xia conferred and thought that returning early would only lead to new tasks; there really was no need to rush back; they might as well stay and watch the competition before returning.

Although they didn’t understand the Spirit Chef Competition, they also wanted to witness Lu Yang’s legendary performance.

"Except for Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, who will win, the situations of the other four groups seem worrisome."

Jin Tan only needed to exchange four ingredients to create his ultimate dish.

"No matter, I see a promising young fellow in the Two Star Spirit Chef Team over there." Daoist Ming Yuan smiled, seemingly unconcerned about Jin Tan.

Everyone’s attention was focused on the Five Star Spirit Chef Team, with very few noticing the competition within the Two Star Spirit Chef Team.

The Two Star Spirit Chef Team was the first to enter the third round with the dish "Fish but Not Fish".

Young Master Wu looked at the dazed Song Tianjing and secretly snickered.

Do you realize, boy, that the pufferfish you chose has been tainted with my Five Poisons? Even if you have a Poison Immune Body and aren’t affected, can the judges withstand it?

Once the time comes, your reputation as a Spirit Chef will be utterly ruined, with no chance of redemption, and I will emerge victorious and win the beauty!

Blame yourself for offending this young master!

Song Tianjing indeed realized that his pufferfish had been poisoned by Young Master Wu, but his daze was not due to contemplating how to break out of this predicament but rather pondering whether this was a dream or reality.

The events in the dream were unfolding one by one; the previous experience seemed more like a premonition of the future rather than just a dream.

Could it be that revealing possession of the "Culinary Bible" would lead to being hunted by the Spirit Chef Alliance?

Even though in the future, he would evade the pursuit, obtain the entire inheritance of the Complete Culinary Compendium, defeat the leader of the Spirit Chef Alliance, and become the new leader, during the pursuit, Qian’er would tragically be poisoned, his younger brother would take a blade for him, the elder brother, who initially pursued him but was later swayed by him, lost an arm in the battle against the Spirit Chef Alliance, and although they escaped, his sworn brothers could not evade their fated doom...

"As long as I’m not being hunted by the Spirit Chef Alliance, I can avoid all these futures!"

"I need to rewrite the future!"

"A keen look indeed," Daoist Ming Yuan remarked.

Although he didn’t understand why Song Tianjing wore a look that suggested he was ready to make a noble sacrifice.

The first recipe in the "Complete Culinary Compendium" is called Pearl Fish Soup, which primarily requires fish and Five Poisons; Master Wu’s act of poisoning the fish actually aided Song Tianjing.

The second dish, Eight Treasure Chicken Duck Fish, required the fish bones from the Pearl Fish Soup as a starter to bring out the full flavor of the dish.

But now, he couldn’t exactly follow the recipes for Eight Treasure Chicken Duck Fish, even resemblances might arouse suspicion!

By gaining the Forbidden Book, he had made himself an enemy of the Spirit Chef Alliance, a case of gaining some and losing some.

The Eight Treasure Chicken Duck Fish required thirty-six ingredients and had an extremely intricate and complex production process; he needed to boldly modify the recipe!

Oh ancestors of the Yangyuan Building, bless your descendants!

If the ancestors could use the incomplete "Complete Culinary Compendium" to recreate some dishes, then he could use the "Complete Culinary Compendium" to restore some dishes!

Why shouldn’t modern people be as good as the ancients?

In the Spirit Chef Alliance, flame control skills are divided into five levels: Beginner, Proficient, Minor Achievement, Major Achievement, and Consummation.

As Song Tianjing’s cultivation level advanced to the Foundation Establishment Late Stage, his skill in controlling flames underwent a transformation, reaching the Proficient level!

With one hand, Song Tianjing controlled the flames, making the fish soup thick and white, while with the other, he finely chopped the ingredients to better enhance the flavors!

When the last grain of sand in the hourglass fell, Song Tianjing finally completed the Three Treasure Chicken Duck Fish.

Master Wu was the second to last to finish; he had absolute confidence in his own abilities; Song Tianjing couldn’t beat him!

He lifted the lid of the serving dish, revealing a dazzling light; as the light dissipated, what lay in front of the five judges were small golden ingots.

Some of the five judges were professional Spirit Chefs, some were gourmets, and others were ordinary people; they picked up a golden ingot, their eyes widening in amazement.

"It’s a deep-fried dumpling!"

"No, it’s more than just that; his dumpling wrapper isn’t made of flour, it’s made of fish skin!"

"The filling is a mix of squid bits and pork filling, the latter making up a small part serving as a binder!"

"Fish yet not fish; it truly is fish yet not fish!"

Master Wu, with a humble smile, introduced, "This is the Golden Fish Skin Dumpling I made!"

"Golden Fish Skin Dumplings, indeed quite impressive."

All five judges nodded in agreement; this was clearly a notch above the first three dishes!

Song Tianjing lifted his serving dish lid, revealing an entire old duck, though it lacked the luster of Master Wu’s presentation.

"This is the Three Treasures Ruyi Soup I made."

Song Tianjing sliced the old duck open to reveal the old hen wrapped inside; the fragrance was compelling, tapping into the judges’ cravings.

They hurriedly took a sip of the soup, their expressions turning to surprise; Master Wu smirked, guessing they had realized they were poisoned.

Yet, to Master Wu’s astonishment, the judges, who had only sampled a bite from the first four dishes, began to sip one spoon after another, increasingly faster!

The judges closed their eyes, savoring the soup’s impact and satisfaction.

They felt surrounded by the energetic presence of chicken, duck, and fish; even though the fish weren’t visible, the fish’s fragrance leisurely infused into the soup, spreading in their mouths, their blood turning as salty as the sea, countless fish swimming within!

The leading judge, the champion of the previous two-star Spirit Chef competition, nodded along with the four others. Not a word was needed to reach a unanimous decision.

He stood up to announce the result.

"I announce, the champion of the Two Star Spirit Chef Team is Song Tianjing!"

On the sleeve of Song Tianjing’s arm, two black stars were covered by glaring gold!

Chapter 1100: Chapter 199: Tofu Showdown!

Due to Lu Yang’s appearance, the Five Star Spirit Chef Team garnered much attention, with even those originally intending to watch the Seven Star Spirit Chef Team being lured over in significant numbers. freēnovelkiss.com

"Who would’ve thought that Lu Yang is a Spirit Chef with Immortal Chef’s Successor’s inheritance!" Xie Qi stared intensely at Lu Yang, mimicking his every move.

So what if he has received the Immortal Chef’s inheritance? I will prove to the world that not only can I imitate the dishes of the Immortal Chef’s Successor, but I can even improve upon them!

Xie Qi touched the vials and jars strapped to his waist, revealing a smile filled with deep meaning.

These were his secret weapons, containing spices he had collected from his travels across the Cultivation World, especially from Buddha Country.

The Spirit Chef World overlooked Buddha Country, even excluding it from their ranks, yet Xie Qi discovered that while Buddha Country’s dishes were indescribably poor, or rather unpalatable, its spices were unmatched by any other place.

With the power of these spices, he could make any dish taste even better!

An Tong also longed to compete with Lu Yang on the same stage and see who the better chef was!

The "Invincible" An Tong, as the outside world called her, had never lost since her debut. Lu Yang would not be an exception!

As the center of attention, Lu Yang felt there was no need for everyone to keep looking at him this way.

He had only practiced his knife skills for a few days, followed Fairy Eternity in recognizing some odd Spiritual Plants, which he hadn’t even used yet.

As for cooking, he was a complete novice—what could he rely on to win?

He might as well casually prepare something and let Xie Qi and An Tong fight over first place.

After all, he didn’t care whether Jin Tan’s side would win or not. This was an internal struggle of the Spirit Chef Alliance, and he was just an observer.

Liu Xing spread his arms wide, and the outermost walls of the examination area collapsed, revealing rows upon rows of ingredients—birds, beasts, Spirit Beans, Spirit Rice, everything one could wish for.

He announced the final challenge loud and clear, "For the Five Star Spirit Chef Team, the last challenge is to make a dish using tofu!"

Lu Yang: "..."

Lu Yang, clutching his forehead in pain, first thought of his early Cultivation days, when Eldest Senior Sister made him practice Swordsmanship with tofu. He had to chop as much tofu by day as he would then have to eat at meals, and at night, even his nightmares were haunted by Tofu Heavenly Venerate, to the point where he felt nauseated at the sight of tofu.

Do you Spirit Chefs even want positive coverage anymore?

"Little Yang, go for it! My recipe includes a Yin Yang Tofu. Let them see the level of Immortal cooking!" Fairy Eternity egged on.

Lu Yang’s eye twitched as he had translated the entire Complete Culinary Compendium, resulting in his ability to remember the preparation method for every single dish listed.

The Imperial edict was inviolable—what right did a subject have to resist His Majesty’s decree?

Lu Yang begrudgingly started making the Yin Yang Tofu.

As the name implied, Yin Yang Tofu consisted of tofu in two colors, black and white. To achieve this, one needed hundreds of black and white ingredients to create a composite sauce to dye the tofu.

Black foods like squid ink, soy sauce, and more.

White foods like salt, sugar, and more.

"Fairy, wouldn’t this make it too salty?"

"Don’t worry, just add some chili pepper at the end, it will balance out the saltiness!"

"This Yin Yang Tofu embodies the Yin Yang Path, it contains endless worlds, and its wonders are infinite. If you manage to comprehend this aspect, you will have entered the threshold of the Yin Yang Path..." Fairy Eternity rambled on and on, recounting her philosophy behind creating this dish.

Xie Qi kept pace with Lu Yang’s actions, pouring hundreds of vials and jars together and mixing them thoroughly.

Watching the black and white mixture unwittingly react and bubble, Xie Qi began to doubt whether Lu Yang was truly an Immortal Chef’s Successor.

But recalling all the rumors about Lu Yang, he gritted his teeth, believed, and continued to follow the recipe!

Staring at the ball-shaped slices of tofu doused in the sauce, Xie Qi’s index finger twitched in anticipation.

Although the cooking process was inexplicably mysterious, the finished product smelled incredibly fragrant!

"Let me taste it and see what faults this tofu has."

Xie Qi took a spoonful and incredulously clutched his throat, making "uh-uh" sounds.

Two extreme flavors collided in his mouth. His taste sense, already far superior to a normal person’s, was amplified to an unbearable degree by the effect. These flavors tormented him to an extent that life seemed worse than death.

Clang—

Xie Qi collapsed to the ground, foaming at the mouth and lost to unconsciousness.

Without employing a single soldier, Lu Yang had forced Xie Qi out of the competition. This could truly be called a masterstroke strategy, winning without fighting!

The final matchup came down to Lu Yang and An Tong.

"Time’s up!" Liu Xing declared loudly.

"Considering Xie Qi’s withdrawal due to unforeseen circumstances, after discussion by the alliance’s higher-ups, we’ve decided to adopt a different method for this competition’s evaluation!"

"We will switch to each side tasting the other’s dishes and giving scores!"

Lu Yang presented the Yin Yang Tofu, drenched in brilliant red chili oil, while An Tong presented tofu in the shape of an orange.

"Now, let’s begin the tasting."

Lu Yang examined An Tong’s orange-shaped tofu, which was coated in a shell resembling a sugar glaze. With a gentle tap of his spoon, Lu Yang cracked the sugar shell, revealing the white and bouncy tofu inside.

Taking a spoonful of both sugar coating and tofu, Lu Yang tasted it. The originally bland tofu became enriched in flavor with the addition of an orange essence, and mixing in bamboo shoots gave the tofu a particularly crisp bite.

This flavor was leaps and bounds beyond Fairy Eternity’s creations!

While Lu Yang savored An Tong’s orange tofu, An Tong was also studying Lu Yang’s Yin Yang Tofu.

As a child, a high fever had taken her sense of taste, but it had also led to an abnormal development of her vision, touch, smell, and hearing.

"The layer of red oil on this Yin Yang Tofu is visually striking without overpowering the tofu’s fragrance. The black and white tofu has not only the aroma of tofu but also combines scents from the sea, the sky, and the earth."

She didn’t even need to taste it to know that it was a superb tofu that completely overshadowed her own orange tofu!

It was a true masterpiece of tofu!

Although she lacked the sense of taste, An Tong still wanted to try a bite—out of respect for Lu Yang.

Just as Lu Yang was about to advise An Tong not to eat it, ready to concede defeat, he saw An Tong take a spoonful of the Yin Yang Tofu. Gripping her neck and wide-mouthed, she shouted an evaluation, louder than she ever had in her life.

"So spicy, so salty!!"

"How can it be this spicy!"

An Tong gulped down water, which finally lowered the temperature in her mouth a bit and allowed her to calm down, contemplating more deeply.

"Wait, do I now have a sense of taste?!"

"I—I have my sense of taste back?"

An Tong devoured the Yin Yang Tofu with tears dripping onto the plate, sobbing with a smile, "Delicious, it’s really delicious..."

After a while, An Tong finally calmed her inner turmoil and bowed deeply to Lu Yang. "Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, you have won, I concede defeat voluntarily."

Though she was on Jin Tan’s side, she had her own principles. Lu Yang had saved her sense of taste with his tofu—how could she be qualified to judge Lu Yang’s Yin Yang Tofu?

Saying so, she left the stage without awaiting Lu Yang’s reaction, leaving behind a bewildered Lu Yang.

Even as Liu Xing announced the results and Lu Yang’s sleeve was adorned with five golden stars, denoting his status as the strongest among the Five Star Spirit Chefs, he hadn’t snapped back to reality.

Wait, how did I just win with these skills?

Chapter 1102: Chapter 1101: Falling into a Trap!

The edict represented Zhu Tian’s personal involvement, demanding reverence.

Merely an illusion, merely five words, yet they made two Transcendance Tribulation Cultivators cease their hostilities, not daring to harbor any covetous thoughts, illustrating the profound authority of Zhu Tian!

What talk is there of punishment? Just ensure that you two do not fight within Demon City, lest it disturbs the lives of the citizens."

His gaze was profound, as if gazing into the Dragon and Phoenix battles of ancient times, yet also seeming concerned about the current livelihood of Demon City’s citizens, merging past and present in an inscrutable manner.

"Yes."

"Thank you, Nation Master Zhu."

The illusion of Zhu Tian dissipated, the edict returning to the Imperial Palace by carriage, the golden path also vanished into the sky, turning into golden light like numerous stars, resonating beautifully with the sunset.

Throughout this process, Daoist Ming Yuan continued to show his respect towards Zhu Tian by bowing deeply without once raising his head.

Outside of Demon City, a series of Array Methods that had been buried illuminated one after another, silently spreading throughout the entire city, isolating it from external contact temporarily, turning Demon City into a self-contained small world.

Daoist Ming Yuan spoke respectfully to the jade pendant hanging on his chest shaped like an eye.

The shadow sitting on the throne of bones stood up, took a step forward, and vanished from the jade pendant’s small world, appearing right in front of Yun Mengmeng.

"Yun Mengmeng, you fell into the trap after all!" the shadow said with a faint smile, its body trembling slightly with uncontrollable excitement.

He, driven to obtain the Initial Form of Immortal Dao Fruit, had the power to flee from the Silent Extermination Immortal. He had set his sights on Yun Mengmeng’s Initial Form of Immortal Dao Fruit.

But Yun Mengmeng was at the Seek Dao Sect and Seek Dao Sect had Yun Zhi, so it was absolutely impossible to take action there.

Therefore, he found out that Yun Mengmeng referred to Lu Yang as the second-in-command and had a deep connection with Lu Yang, and also learned that Yun Mengmeng enjoyed good food. So, he ordered Daoist Ming Yuan to open the Spirit Chef Competition in Demon City and invited Lu Yang to come.

If Lu Yang came, Yun Mengmeng would surely follow!

So, he also had Daoist Ming Yuan set up a Great Formation in Demon City, allowing it to become a self-contained small world, isolated from the Silent Extermination Immortal’s sensing.

In this way, he could act without any hesitation!

Setting up such a formation was difficult; Daoist Ming Yuan spent more than ten days completing it.

Everything went according to his plan, Lu Yang accepted the invitation and came, with Yun Mengmeng following.

The Initial Form of Immortal Dao Fruit was right before his eyes!

Chapter 1103: Chapter 1102: She’s Doing Well With Me

Lu Yang stood frozen in place, his forehead covered in a dense layer of sweat beads.

Why on earth was Ashy Bean here, and why had she come looking for him directly?!

Lu Yang noticed that the passersby were oblivious to Ashy Bean’s presence, and by extension, they ignored his existence as well.

Was this the characteristic of nearing Transcendence that Eldest Senior Sister and Fairy had mentioned about Ashy Bean?

He suspected that if Ashy Bean hadn’t wanted to know the whereabouts of Fairy Eternity, she would have killed him in the instant they met!

Ashy Bean had been able to sense his presence all along; why had she only come looking for him now? Had something changed, or did Ashy Bean have a compelling reason to find him?

Lu Yang and Ashy Bean locked eyes, his gaze as serene as an ancient well. Despite bearing the same visage as Fairy Eternity, she imparted a completely different feeling to Lu Yang.

Ashy Bean had no interest in Lu Yang; whether he was the foremost of the Geniuses in this world or someone who had defeated Si Chen God Lord with an Immortal Body, none of it mattered to her. She just wanted to know the whereabouts of Immortal Fairy.

Instinct told Ashy Bean that finding Lu Yang would lead her to Immortal Fairy.

"Senior, perhaps we could change locations..."

"Can you imagine what I felt at that time? One moment, I was on the verge of becoming an Immortal, the first Immortal in history, and the next moment, I found myself a hundred thousand years later, possessing an Immortal Body, and becoming the supreme Heavenly Court Master."

Hearing the familiar name, Fairy Eternity’s expression shifted.

Chapter 1104: Chapter 1103: Zuo Shi Immortal’s Luck

Over the years, he had been hiding here and there, avoiding the perception of Silent Extermination Immortal. Today, in order to make a move, he had planned for a long time to ensure that Silent Extermination Immortal couldn’t sense him, and only then did he come out from the Small World.

Chapter 1107: Chapter 1106: The False Past

Time Immortal thus persuaded you to give up the Annihilation Dao Fruit and switch to the Eternity Dao Fruit, intending to trap you in this event, preventing you from becoming immortal. Unexpectedly, you let go of your obsession and formed the Eternity Dao Fruit, making them envious and murderous towards you. That’s why they cruelly attacked you!"

"Hey Little Lotus, you were wrong, I have a name, my name is Ashy Bean..."

Qinghe hurriedly reached out to grab Ashy Bean, but her figure had already dissipated into specks of light in the air, leaving nothing to grasp.

Chapter 1111: Chapter 1110: Return to the Sect

Spreading his empty hands, Qinghe felt a sense of melancholy as if something had been lost.

So, the boss who forced himself to stay by his side for three hundred thousand years had finally left?

Now that he no longer needed to stay by Ashy Bean’s side and had finally gained his freedom, Qinghe didn’t feel any relief or joy. Instead, his heart felt hollow and carried an indescribable aftertaste.

"Cough cough cough—" Fairy Eternity started coughing violently. The battle hadn’t been easy; her Immortal Power suppressed the Power of Silence, and the Power of Silence likewise restrained the Immortal Power.

Looking at the battered Fairy Eternity, Lu Yang’s heart tightened.

Previously, Fairy Eternity had been an Immortal Soul, intangible, and this was the first time Lu Yang had touched Fairy Eternity’s body, but it was under such circumstances.

The farewell from the Fairy just before was like a last goodbye, scaring Lu Yang out of his wits.

Fairy Eternity had delayed regenerating her Immortal Body but had forcibly done so during the battle, undoubtedly at a irreversible cost.
