Her body gradually dissipated and once again became a soul, sliding into Lu Yang’s Spiritual Space. She lay down skillfully on the bed, and her voice, weak as a thread, came from it.

"I originally needed a hundred years to recover my Immortal Body, but now that I’ve forced its recovery, it might take two hundred years to fully recover. Little Yang, I’ll be bothering you for a bit longer..."

"No trouble at all, as long as you’re fine, you can stay as long as you want!" Lu Yang quickly said, as long as Fairy Eternity was fine, anything was acceptable.

Qinghe, Yun Mengmeng, and Jin Caiwei all breathed a sigh of relief. It was good that there was no serious issue.

Qinghe’s mind flashed with a question. Why did the chief need to stay in Lu Yang’s Spiritual Space? Seeing that Yun Mengmeng and Jin Caiwei didn’t react much, could it be that the chief had always been staying there before this?

"It’s, it’s over, right?"

Zhu Tian timidly asked himself in a whisper, the battle having truly frightened him, even bringing the thought of going back to sleep.

Originally, he chose to sleep during the Ancient Times because he witnessed the Four Ancient Immortals battling the hidden mastermind, thinking it too dangerous back then. Sleeping for a few hundred thousand years, he figured the world would calm down by the time he awoke.

Yet, as luck would have it, he woke up to the same level of battle happening right above his head, almost claiming his dear life.

"No, no, I am the Chosen One who initiated the struggle of the Great Era; if I were to sleep now, wouldn’t I miss this great conflict?"

Zhu Tian was actually enjoying his current life; he was the publicly recognized ruler of the Demon Territory, the revered Demon Emperor—a status he couldn’t enjoy during the Ancient Times.

At most, it was just bad luck, establishing the Demon Nation when Jiang Lianyi awakened, and now again coinciding with the battle between two immortals.

Wait a second, how come every time something happens, Elder Brother Lu Yang is present?

"Zhu Tian, what happened here, who was just fighting, and where is Demon City?"

"Hello, Sister Jiang, hello, Sister Ao."

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi happened to be in the Demon Territory, sensing the terrifying battle that erupted in Demon City, they quickly rushed to investigate. However, by the time they arrived, the battle had ended, and the vast Demon City had vanished without a trace, leaving only Zhu Tian muttering to himself.

"It’s Elder Brother Lu Yang!" The two women had sharp eyes and immediately spotted Lu Yang at the site where Demon City used to be; they didn’t even bother to ask Zhu Tian and flew over directly.

"Miss Qinghe is here too!" Seeing Qinghe, whom they had not seen for over three hundred thousand years, brought the two women great joy.

"Sister Ling, Sister Lianyi."

The arrival of the two women dispelled the depressing atmosphere at the scene. Qinghe had heard about the awakening of Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi early on but was too tied up to leave.

"What happened just now?"

After hearing Lu Yang’s account, the two women couldn’t help but feel nostalgic. Ao Ling was more touched than Jiang Lianyi, who had slept early and was unaware of the affairs of the Fire Dynasty and Ashy Bean. It was after the establishment of the Fire Dynasty that Ao Ling had gone to sleep.

"Is Immortal Sister alright?"

Lu Yang glanced at Fairy Eternity, who was lying in bed asleep in the Spiritual Space, and replied, "She’s fine, just sleeping."

Just didn’t know what kind of dream Fairy Eternity was having, her lips curved in a smile.

Fairy Eternity stealthily opened one eye, confirming Little Yang had left, and then went back to sleep.

"The techniques of the Timeless Immortal Sect really do work."

"What do you plan to do now?" asked Jiang Lianyi.

"Return to the Sect."

"Then we will go back with you."

Jiang Lianyi and Ao Ling decided to follow, after such a significant event, they certainly could not just leave after finding out what happened; moreover, Qinghe was bound to accompany them to Seek Dao Sect, and it would be a good opportunity to catch up along the way.

"How should we deal with Daoist Ming Yuan?" Yun Mengmeng inquired, as the battle had begun with Daoist Ming Yuan being flattened by Jin Caiwei and left in Demon City.

Lu Yang pondered for a moment, thinking Captive Peak could handle one more or one less at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage; the fight had been a bolt from the blue for Demon City, and Zhu Tian indeed had it hard. He decided to leave Daoist Ming Yuan to Zhu Tian, after all, a Demon Emperor paired with an Eighth Star Spirit Chef would have some prestige when spoken about.

"Daoist Ming Yuan is left to Zhu Tian to handle, let’s go home," Lu Yang called out.

Before departing, Jin Caiwei restored Demon City to its original state.

On the way home, Lu Yang was surrounded, with Yun Mengmeng on his left hand side, and Ao Ling, Jiang Lianyi, Qinghe, and Jin Caiwei on his right, all chatting and laughing.

Seems like he was the only one not a Semi-Immortal?

Lu Yang, escorted by five Semi-Immortals, arrived at Seek Dao Sect, a reception not even the Four Ancient Immortals had enjoyed, such a prestigious welcome truly warranted Eldest Senior Sister’s personal reception at the gate.

"Eldest Senior Sister..." Seeing Eldest Senior Sister, Lu Yang felt like he had found his pillar, and was extremely excited.

"Xiao Zhi, we are back!" Yun Mengmeng greeted her cheerily. This trip had indeed been quite an eye-opener.

"Miss Yun, cough cough, to think that I would live to see you again..." Immortal Fairy awoke and floated out from the Spiritual Space.

Seeing Immortal Fairy weakened and disheveled, Yun Zhi showed a puzzled expression on her face. She opened her mouth, but in the end, she held back what she wanted to say.

Chapter 1112: Chapter 1111 Eye Contact

Long ago, Yun Zhi had already realized that Fairy Eternity could restore her immortal body at any time, yet she stubbornly remained in Junior Brother’s spiritual space and refused to leave.

As Fairy Eternity was a senior, Yun Zhi couldn’t just kick her out without giving her face, so Yun Zhi thought to wait until Junior Brother encountered danger, trusting that the senior would intervene and then would have no reason to stay in the spiritual space.

Each time Lu Yang encountered danger and couldn’t call for Yun Zhi, she did not prepare any life-saving measures for him afterward, precisely because of this reason.

Unexpectedly, in these few instances, there was no need for the senior to make a move, and Junior Brother remained safe and sound.

Yun Zhi had originally thought that since Grey Immortal’s strength was formidable, Fairy Eternity wouldn’t be able to defeat her without restoring her immortal body. Now it seems the immortal body was restored, and then it disappeared again?

Fairy Eternity gave Yun Zhi a glance, and Yun Zhi also looked back at Fairy Eternity; everything was communicated through their eyes.

Yun Zhi felt a headache coming on—sure enough, out of all things in this world, only cultivation was truly worry-free.

"This isn’t a place to talk; everybody, please come in."

Yun Zhi invited everyone to Sky Gate Mountain, where the four Emperor’s Chairs now seemed too few.

"Let’s just sit on the ground," Yun Mengmeng suggested to everyone, finding a spot in the shade, she pulled out a camping blanket and spread it on the ground.

She then took out all the delicious foods she had tasted in the market from her storage ring, carefully selected and doubly approved by her and Qinghe as delectable, specifically brought back for Xiao Zhi to try.

By sharing with everyone, it was roughly the same as Xiao Zhi having a taste.

As everyone was familiar with each other, there was no need for formalities. Lu Yang picked up a long pastry he had never seen before, crispy on the outside, with surprisingly a meat filling inside—delicious.

Lu Yang had only visited the market on the first day, spending the rest of his time in seclusion, honing his culinary skills within the Qiongqi Clan, and had not completed his tour of the market’s delicacies.

"Pastries like these are better when heated," Yun Mengmeng mentioned, having grown into an exceptional gourmet during the few short years since joining Yun Zhi.

Lu Yang readily agreed and used the Three Flavored True Fire to heat the pastry, indeed improving the taste to another level, making it even crispier, and the meat filling’s juice burst out.

Good things were meant to be shared. Lu Yang tossed a ball of Three Flavored True Fire into the air for anyone to use if they wished.

It was then that the group began to debrief the events that had transpired.

Yun Zhi ate as she listened, nodding frequently—the main reason being that after she finished a piece, her good friend would immediately stuff another one into her hand.

"So Grey Immortal had such an experience."

Yun Zhi also sighed, but knew this was the only outcome.

Grey Immortal’s strength was undeniable; even when Fairy Senior clashed with her, she dared not hold back. It was extremely difficult to capture her alive, and with Grey Immortal’s temperament, she probably wouldn’t allow herself to be taken alive.

Approaching transcendence, Yun Zhi had yet to deal with such a person before and was eager to understand more about the realm of Transcendence.

"How did the mastermind behind the scenes show Zuo Shi Immortal the past exactly? Was it based on reasonable assumptions?"

Yun Zhi’s brow furrowed, meddling with the Insight Dao Fruit; this already surpassed the capabilities of the Cause and Effect Dao Fruit.

"Could it be that the mastermind has more than one Dao Fruit?"

But that seemed impossible, in theory, only the Dao Fruit of the devouring lineage can merge with other Dao Fruits, and the Devouring Dao Fruit belongs to Mid-heaven Emperor Lord.

Dao Fruits are unique. If the mastermind had the Devouring Dao Fruit, then the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord couldn’t possibly have it.

"What are Qinghe Senior’s plans for the future?"

"Wherever my lord goes, I shall follow," Qinghe stated firmly, determined to continue in the footsteps of her lord.

As she said these words, Qinghe watched Lu Yang vigilantly, resolute in not allowing her lord to be tainted by such a person again!

Lu Yang didn’t quite understand why Qinghe, his senior, looked at him with such a gaze, as if she had some hostility towards him from the moment she first saw him.

Hearing that Qinghe was the Fairy Eternity’s first devotee and most devout, could it be because he wasn’t good enough to the fairy?

Lu Yang felt that he had been good enough to the fairy, taking charge, keeping her company, accepting tests, possessing at will, and even listening to her shameful past...

Forget it, he no longer wanted to think about it. She had taken Fairy Eternity as her faith; it was normal for him not to understand her thoughts.

"By the way, Little Lotus, do you know where my North Star has gone?"

The North Star was the only celestial body under Fairy Eternity’s control, buried with countless Immortal Treasures of immeasurable value. Fairy Eternity still remembered promising Little Yang that once they found the North Star, he could establish his own faction and wield power.

After the mastermind behind the scenes killed Fairy Eternity, people forgot her existence, including Qinghe.

But she clearly remembered the North Star, Twin River, and Mother-child River were very important to her, so she took the opportunity when the Four Ancient Immortals and the mastermind were battling to move these things away.

"The North Star has been moved outside the box world by me," Qinghe said, feeling ashamed. She moved the North Star to a place far from the center of the battle, so far that it wasn’t even included when the Four Immortals created the box world.

"No worries, no worries. With Little Yang here, we’ll be able to open the box world sooner or later," Fairy Eternity said nonchalantly, not taking the matter too seriously.

"Fairy, it’s not me who opened the box world. I saw it opened," Lu Yang corrected earnestly, as he didn’t have such great power.

"It’s all the same."

"Will the box world open?" Ao Ling, Jiang Lianyi, and Jin Caiwei asked, their eyes gleaming with excitement.

Although the box world was vast, the stars of Ancient Times were also magnificent, and they missed the dazzling stellars cape of that era very much.

Of course, the number of stars they had shattered was also not small.

"I’ve only seen a glimpse of the future; it doesn’t necessarily mean it’s true," Lu Yang added, explaining that even the Time Immortal said the future was uncertain, to prevent the three women from getting their hopes up in vain should the box world remain closed.

"Little Lotus, do you want to join our Immortal Lineage?" Yun Mengmeng asked, believing that it was best for the Immortal Lineage to grow stronger, and considering Little Lotus’s possession of the Longevity Dao Fruit Embryo made her partly of their lineage.

"Little Lotus, join the Immortal Lineage, and you can be the Third Boss!" Fairy Eternity said with a giggling smile. Sha Meless, who had toiled hard with conscientiousness for so many years and had been promoted to Fourth Housekeeper without any complaints, ought to be promoted to a Fifth Housekeeper by now.

Qinghe waved her hands frantically, humbly replying, "I have dull talents, how can I be qualified to join your lineage?"

Lu Yang thought to himself, ’Dull talents, does that mean you’ve cultivated your Longevity Dao Fruit Embryo to consummation?’

Qinghe had not refused to join the Immortal Lineage for the first time. Since Ancient Times, she had felt unworthy of Fairy Eternity and had declined the proposal. She still felt the same way now.

"Come on, join!"

Qinghe firmly refused Fairy Eternity’s offer.

"Then join our Great Bean Dynasty!" Yun Mengmeng continued to pitch her affiliated power with great dedication.

"The Great Bean Dynasty?" Qinghe wondered, as she had never heard of this force.

"It’s a dynasty established by the Chief Housekeeper, quite impressive! I am the Minister of Rites, Ao Ling is the Great General, Emperor Xia is the Prime Minister, and the Second-in-command is the Pillar Nation Minister!"

"A dynasty established by the Chief Housekeeper?" Qinghe was astounded and somewhat touched. She hadn’t expected the Chief Housekeeper to be able to establish this great power spanning the Demon Territory, East Sea, and Central Continent without her help.

"I’ll join!"

"What position do you want to hold?" Fairy Eternity asked. In their Great Bean Dynasty, there was no shortage of idle official positions, and one could choose any upon joining.

"Historian."

Chapter 1113: Chapter 112: The Holy Body is Unwell

"Fine, then I hereby appoint you as the historian of our dynasty to record the affairs of our era!"

Fairy Eternity placed great emphasis on ceremony, referring to herself as "I, the sovereign" when appointing Qinghe, instantly transforming and donning an imperial robe embroidered with her own image on the front and that of Eldest Senior Sister on the back.

"Thank you, Your Majesty!"

"Come, come, let’s celebrate." Yun Mengmeng invited everyone to raise their glasses; the Great Bean Dynasty had gained another great general, truly a cause for celebration.

Yun Zhi hesitated about whether to join in with a toast; it seemed that everyone here, except herself, was a member of the Great Bean Dynasty.

However, it appeared that Fairy Senior had not noticed this point and proposed to recruit her to the Great Bean Dynasty as well.

Better not to draw too much attention and let the Fairy remember herself; just go with the flow.

Everyone raised their glasses in celebration of the mounting power of the Great Bean Dynasty, all in joyful harmony.

"Ms. Qinghe, have you always lived in Lu Yang’s Spiritual Space?" asked Qinghe, who had been holding back all this time, but ultimately couldn’t resist.

"Not at all, ever since I revived, I’ve lived right here, and it’s been so comfortable."

Speaking of Spiritual Space, Fairy Eternity’s eyes danced with excitement, and she gesticulated wildly, though it was unclear what she was miming; suddenly remembering her grievous injuries, she quickly coughed several times.

"Come, come, come, my beloved subjects, come visit my Spiritual Space."

"Fairy, this is my Spiritual Space," Lu Yang reminded her.

"Then let’s all visit my and Little Yang’s Spiritual Space."

"..."

Although Lu Yang always insisted that it was his Spiritual Space, Fairy Eternity just had to think about it, and she could open the gates to let everyone in at their leisure, leaving Lu Yang with no choice but to stare helplessly.

"What a beautiful palace," Yun Mengmeng marveled, looking up and around in genuine wonder.

"Indeed, it’s quite nice," Yun Zhi added, nodding. Though the taste of Fairy Senior’s imperial robe was debatable, her taste in palace construction was certainly commendable.

Known for its beauty, copied from the Great Xia Palace.

Lu Yang’s Spiritual Space could be said to be the heart of the Great Bean Dynasty, with the Soybean Imperial Palace in place, and Fairy Eternity usually resided in the sleeping chambers.

"Ms. Qinghe, why don’t you move into my Spiritual Space? Mine is even bigger!" Qinghe offered with enthusiasm.

"I’d rather not," Fairy Eternity declined without a second thought. It was nice staying in Little Yang’s Spiritual Space, where something fun happened every day, much more interesting than in Ancient Times.

"How about you live here as well?"

The Spiritual Space was vast, having Qinghe would make it more lively.

To be honest, Qinghe was tempted; it would be a good thing to live with Great Fairy, and like in Ancient Times, she could serve her and guard against any mischief from Lu Yang.

But she had her concerns: "What about my body?"

It was safer to keep her body where she could see it.

Fairy Eternity had already thought it through: "That’s simple, the Green Peak Sword possessed by Little Yang contains a Small World. Just temporarily store your body there."

"I’ll follow Great Fairy’s advice!"

Qinghe immediately performed an Astral Projection, leaving her body in the Green Peak Sword Small World, her soul moving into the Spiritual Space. Lu Yang, despite his decisive actions, didn’t even have time to react.

"Can we also live in the Spiritual Space?" Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi, seeing the opportunity, were also tempted.

Fairy Eternity looked at the two women with confusion, "Aren’t you two seeking the Qilin Immortal? Would it be appropriate for you to stay with me?"

"Oh right, we still have to find our husband," the two women remembered the matter of the Qilin Immortal in their joy, almost forgetting it.

Fairy Eternity led everyone on a tour of the Soybean Imperial Palace, where every brick and tile had been built by her, far surpassing the Great Xia Palace in grandeur.

After the tour, Yun Mengmeng volunteered, "Chief Housekeeper, since our Great Bean Dynasty has gained a new general, should we challenge Xiao Zhi again?"

She too was a loyal servant of the Great Bean Dynasty, intent on achieving meritorious service.

Although she and Xiao Zhi were as close as sisters, being in two opposing camps now, she had no choice but to set aside their past friendship!

"Do, do we have to fight?" Jin Caiwei clutched her clothes tightly, looking around nervously to gauge everyone’s reaction. The previous fight with Yun Zhi, where she was defeated as easily as chopping vegetables, left her with quite a psychological shadow.

Lu Yang, listening to the side, had his eyebrows twitching. Sister Mengmeng, could you not bring up what should not be discussed?

Fairy Eternity’s eyes lit up when she heard this idea, but then dimmed again. She shook her head calmly and steadily; although the Great Bean Dynasty had grown, it was not the best time to go to war.

"Cough cough, with my cultivation level, I would be able to battle Miss Yun," she regretted. "Unfortunately, I am seriously wounded at the moment and unable to cultivate for battle. We shall let Miss Yun off just this once."

Lu Yang beat his thigh in frustration, showing his loyalty, "We’ve missed a great opportunity! Our Great Bean Dynasty is flourishing, the perfect time to wage war on all fronts. Although my cultivation level is modest, I am willing to work tirelessly for His Majesty, to be the vanguard on the battlefield. It’s such a pity!"

Lu Yang stole a glance at Eldest Senior Sister, who was expressionless.

He believed that with Eldest Senior Sister’s wisdom, she would certainly see that although he resided in the Great Bean Dynasty, his heart had always been with Eldest Senior Sister. She would not blame him.

"Right, it’s such a pity," Yun Mengmeng thought the last time had been rather fun.

Lu Yang, fearing Yun Mengmeng would come up with another terrifying idea, hurriedly helped Fairy Eternity back to the palace.

"His Majesty is not in good health. It’s time to return to the palace to rest."

"In a while, I must report the war situation to Senior Ying Tian."

Everyone left the Spiritual Space and returned to their respective places. Those who were to stay at the Seek Dao Sect stayed there, those who were to return to the Demon Territory stayed, and those who were to go back to the East Sea stayed.

Lu Yang could tell that Ao Ling and the other two women had decided to stay at the Seek Dao Sect for a while.

After all, Senior Qinghe was here; it was time they remained to reminisce.

He set out for Laurel Fairy Palace to retrieve the Black Ancient Ring from Senior Sister Jinghong.

Venerable Ying Long, as ever, soared in the sky, his dragon eyes fixed on Lu Yang with a piercing gaze, "You indeed came. I was considering sending Jinghong to find out what exactly happened in the Demon Territory. Alas, she’s in the Void Refinement Stage, with her cultivation fluctuating, which makes going out dangerous."

"Brother Ying Tian, long time no see," Qinghe emerged from the Spiritual Space, not expecting that Lu Yang had already found Ying Tian Immortal.

"Qinghe?!" Ying Tian Immortal was surprised; Lu Yang really could bring him surprises every time.

After Lu Yang recounted the events of the battle at Demon City, Ying Tian Immortal fell into a prolonged silence.

Silent Extermination Immortal had become so extreme, and they were partly to blame.

"Senior Ying Tian, now that Ashy Bean has disappeared, you can proclaim your existence to the world," Lu Yang suggested, as Ying Tian Immortal had returned to his ancient state. The reason he had not left the Ancient Ring previously was the threat of Ashy Bean, but now that the threat was gone, he could leave.

Ying Tian Immortal’s dragon head shook, "Now is not the right time."

Lu Yang was startled—had something unforeseen happened to Senior Ying Tian?

"As someone of my status, of course I must choose a moment in the spotlight to announce my return to the world!"

Chapter 1114: Chapter 113: With such a treacherous courtier, how can the Great Bean Dynasty not fall!

Although Ying Tian Immortal temporarily didn’t plan to take action publicly, without Ashy Bean, he was able to leave the Ancient Ring small world.

With his cultivation level, no one would notice him.

Most importantly, he could freely control the power of the Tribulation Dao Fruit and manipulate the Heavenly Tribulation!

Ying Tian Immortal and Qinghe had been separated for three hundred thousand years, each with their own rich experiences.

However, these experiences were somewhat embarrassing to speak of, so there was no need to tell Qinghe.

Although Qinghe often followed Immortal Fairy during the ancient times, witnessing countless scenes of humiliation, her dignity had been lost. By the time of the Fire Dynasty, she was in a position of great power and prestige, desired by all.

Presumably, Qinghe’s impression of him during the hundred thousand years in the Fire Dynasty had already overshadowed the memories of ancient times.

What Ying Tian Immortal didn’t know was that on the way, Lu Yang had already finished telling the story of Ying Tian Immortal’s thirty hundred thousand years of hiding and seeking. Upon meeting Ying Tian Immortal, Qinghe pretended to be unaware of his experiences.

After bidding farewell to Ying Tian Immortal, Lu Yang set out for Buddha Country.

If there was a place Lu Yang enjoyed most these days, it was none other than Buddha Country.

Upon entering Buddha Country, Lu Yang summoned his immortal body, which was condensed from the faith of incense, and drove it with the Immortal Sense of Fairy Eternity.

"This state is most comfortable," he said.

With the immortal body, Lu Yang felt that he could change the world with a single thought, commanding the wind and summoning the rain – he was omnipotent.

"If only Old Meng were in Buddha Country," he thought regretfully. He was in his prime, the opportunity perfect. If Old Meng were here, he could have faced him one-on-one.

"Making grand vows and using the power of incense to condense the Immortal Body, then reinforcing it with the Eternity Dao Fruit Embryo?"

Qinghe was most proficient in the Cultivation method of incense faith. The Incense Fire Dao of the Fire Dynasty was created by her.

Qinghe saw through the origin of Lu Yang’s Immortal Body at a glance and did not stay idle; she sliced the Spirit Fruit into the shape of a little rabbit and offered it to the mouth of Immortal Fairy.

"Amm, delicious," Immortal Fairy opened her mouth and ate the rabbit-shaped Spirit Fruit. It tasted very good, indistinguishable from real Spirit Fruits even though it was transformed by Qinghe.

Immortal Fairy felt that having Little Lotus live in the Spiritual Space was wonderful; Little Yang was good to her, too, but not as attentive as Qinghe, at least not serving her like Little Lotus did.

Seeing this scene, Lu Yang was filled with heartache. As a historian, serving His Majesty in such a manner was demeaning. With such sycophants, how could the Great Bean Dynasty avoid falling!

Yet, His Majesty reveled in this, unaware. If he stated the truth directly, it would likely make His Majesty think it was out of jealousy towards a virtuous minister, leaving a bad impression. He had to find a way to persuade Immortal Fairy over time.

As Lu Yang pondered how to advise Immortal Fairy, he arrived at the Mahavira Hall of the Western Paradise Temple undetected.

The Western Paradise Temple had been rebuilt on the ruins of the old one with an entirely different layout, yet the position of the Mahavira Hall remained the same.

The sand sculpture of Western Paradise Temple that Lu Yang gave to Yun Mengmeng became a rare collector’s item.

Inside the Mahavira Hall, a golden Buddha statue yawned and lay sidelong on the Lotus Platform.

"Kid, you’ve come?"

The Time Immortal was not at all surprised by Lu Yang’s arrival.

"Hey, Time, we’re here."

"I have seen Time Immortal, Senior."

"Brother Time, long time no see."

Towards the end of the Fire Dynasty, after Time Immortal was ambushed, Qinghe knew that Time Immortal had not fallen.

Her Longevity Dao Fruit Embryo’s Upper Dao Fruit was the Time Dao Fruit and the Eternity Dao Fruit, so if Time Immortal fell, she would have sensed the extinction of suppression.

""""

Even though the Time Immortal might have perished, she would not have become an Immortal.

Her becoming an Immortal would mean that the Longevity Dao Fruit replaced both the Time Dao Fruit and the Eternity Dao Fruit, and the great one would never be able to be revived.

"Little Qinghe, it’s been a while since we last met," chuckled the Time Immortal. He’d been leaping through time since the end of the Fire Dynasty, and in his perception, not much time had passed since he last saw Qinghe.

"Please, take a seat."

The Time Immortal brought out three spare Lotus Platforms and invited the three to sit down.

"It seems that Fairy Eternity paid a heavy price to defeat the Silent Extermination Immortal, it could take two or three hundred years for her to recover," remarked the Time Immortal, unable to hold back a sigh upon seeing the weakened state of the Immortal Fairy.

"Cough cough..." The Immortal Fairy suddenly began to cough violently, "But it was worth it to save Little Yang."

"Fairy..." Lu Yang was deeply moved upon hearing this, not expecting to hold such significance in the fairy’s heart.

Lu Yang and the others reminisced for a while before taking their leave of the Time Immortal.

Mainly it was the Immortal Fairy and Qinghe catching up, with Lu Yang merely listening in.

After they left, the Time Immortal’s gaze sharpened as he recalled his last encounter with the Immortal Fairy.

Back then, upon foreseeing her future battle with the Silent Extermination Immortal, she knew she had to restore her physical body. Once her body was restored, there would be no reason for her to remain in the Spiritual Space, and that’s why she sought out Lu Yang for help while he was welcoming Yun Zhi.

After learning about the whole situation, he had helped the Immortal Fairy come up with the current solution.

Before leaving the Western Paradise Temple, Lu Yang also went to visit Xin Ding.

"Is Senior Brother Xin Ding still in seclusion?"

"I heard that as soon as Senior Brother Xin Ding went into seclusion, the number one of the earth list also hurried to seclude himself, worried that the Senior Brother might challenge his position after emerging."

"That’s terrifying."

"Considering Senior Brother Xin Ding’s gentle demeanor in daily interactions, who would have thought he ranks second on the earth list?"

Lu Yang smiled as he heard the monks’ comments about Xin Ding, noting that Xin Ding seemed to be doing quite well in the Western Paradise Temple.

In a single step, Lu Yang arrived at Xin Ding’s place of seclusion. Xin Ding had already concluded this phase of seclusion and was discussing his recent enlightenment’s deficiencies with the Heavenly Vault Saint Master.

It seemed that after he had left, the Heavenly Vault Saint Master of the Heavenly Vault Holy Land from Ancient Times had entered Xin Ding’s Spiritual Space as promised, becoming a support for Xin Ding’s cultivation.

"Hehe, little fellow, your progress in cultivation isn’t too bad, is it?" A golden deity, bathed in golden light and with an indistinct face, appeared before Xin Ding.

"Heavenly Venerate!" Xin Ding never expected to see the Tofu Heavenly Venerable again in his lifetime.

"Greetings, Heavenly Venerate," acknowledged the Heavenly Vault Saint Master, recognizing this being as a true Immortal, with a status far above his own Late Tribulation Stage.

"There’s no need for such formality," Lu Yang emitted a gentle light, which involuntarily relaxed both individuals.

"I was visiting Ying Tian and Time, and just thought I’d drop by to check how your cultivation is going."

"Judging now, your progress in cultivation is acceptable."

Hearing the Heavenly Venerate’s appraisal of him, Xin Ding secretly let out a sigh of relief; he was glad he hadn’t disappointed the Heavenly Venerate.

The Heavenly Vault Saint Master, however, was startled. To visit the Yingtian Immortal and Time Immortal—just who could this Tofu Heavenly Venerable be from Ancient Times?

Best not to ponder, he dared not speculate on the identity of the Heavenly Venerate.

Inside the Spiritual Space, Qinghe gave Lu Yang a sidelong glance: had he learned this from the Yingtian Immortal?

"My lord, just what exactly is this..."

"Heh, he’s a natural, isn’t Little Yang impressive?"

Chapter 1115: Chapter 114 Meng Jingzhou’s Day of Suffering

After reminding Xin Ding to be diligent in his cultivation and the Heavenly Vault Saint Master to fully commit to his role as a teacher, Lu Yang floated away, as if he had never been there at all.

Only Xin Ding and the Heavenly Vault Saint Master were left, staring at each other in confusion.

The power of an Immortal is indeed immeasurable.

Just as Lu Yang was preparing to leave Western Heaven City, he suddenly sensed a familiar presence within the city and revealed a meaningful smile.

...

"Excuse me, sir, what do you mean by ordering the best mush hotpot and then only taking one bite before not eating anymore?" the restaurant owner squinted, blocking the path of the customer who was trying to leave and showing a fierce look.

The customer looked displeased: "If the food you make is unpalatable, can you blame me for not eating it?"

"What do you mean unpalatable? Clearly, you’re just finding an excuse to ruin our reputation!" the restaurant owner retorted angrily.

"What? Someone is dissatisfied with my cooking?" A burly man with dense hair on his arm, as thick as that on his head and dough still clinging to his fingers, came out from the back kitchen.

The restaurant owner proudly introduced him: "Our chef has participated in the Spirit Chef competition before, so I need not say more about his skills, right?"

The argument between the three quickly drew the attention of the surrounding diners. In reality, they also thought that the mush hotpot of this restaurant was mediocre, but given the chef’s reputation, if they said it tasted bad, it would seem like they were the ones lacking taste.

The customer was so frustrated that his teeth itched, and had it not been for the sake of face, he would have dropped his disguise long ago.

"What’s wrong, can’t I say it if it tastes bad?" A resonant voice rang out, echoing through the restaurant.

A tall figure stepped into the restaurant with his back to the sun, and after tasting the mush hotpot, he confirmed it was indeed unpalatable, even more so than the last mush hotpot he had eaten.

"It’s Lu Yang!" the diners exclaimed in surprise at the identity of the newcomer.

The restaurant owner was still in denial and snorted coldly, "So what if it’s Lu Yang? As far as I know, the Seek Dao Sect doesn’t even qualify to participate in the Spirit Chef competition, so what authority does he have to critique our hotpot!"

What the restaurant owner failed to notice was that the chef trembled like a sieve the moment he saw Lu Yang, not daring to look directly into Lu Yang’s eyes.

"Not qualified?"

Unintentionally, Lu Yang loosened the cloth wrapped around his arm, revealing a sleeve embroidered with five golden stars.

"That’s the insignia of a Five Star Spirit Chef!" a diner shouted in shock.

"That’s not right, I’ve seen the insignia of a Five Star Spirit Chef before, and the stars weren’t this color!"

"Ignorant fools, that is the golden constellation insignia, awarded only to those at the pinnacle of Five Star Spirit Chefs!" a seasoned diner scolded.

"What?!"

Lu Yang approached the restaurant owner step by step. Though he released no aura, in the owner’s eyes, Lu Yang seemed like a beast from ancient times, invoking an immense sense of oppression.

"Do I qualify now?"

The restaurant owner numbly nodded his head.

Lu Yang then turned to the trembling chef and asked, "You said you’ve participated in the Spirit Chef competition? Which team were you on, as I haven’t seen you before?"

"I, I was a spectator." The chef had watched from the beginning to the end and knew Lu Yang’s identity, Immortal Chef’s Successor, leader of the Five Star Spirit Chef Team, and dared not hide anything in Lu Yang’s presence.

Lu Yang nodded, knowing there had to be an issue; the Spirit Chef Alliance did not have a chef from the Buddha Country.

Then, Lu Yang beckoned, calling out to his companion, "Old Meng, let’s go."

The two disappeared from everyone’s view.

While returning to the Sect on the way through the great desert, Meng Jingzhou looked at Lu Yang as if he had seen a ghost: "Since when did you become a Five Star Spirit Chef, let alone the leader?"

Those two had known each other for how many years now? What else could Lu Yang, that rascal, do besides grill mutton kebabs?

"It was just showing off a bit during the Spirit Chef competition; I accidentally won," Lu Yang said nonchalantly.

Meng Jingzhou felt that the waters of the Spirit Chef Alliance ran deep.

Seeing Meng Jingzhou maintaining his disguise, Lu Yang, somewhat perplexed, pointed and broke through the disguise, revealing Meng Jingzhou’s shiny bald head with six dots of ordination on top.

Lu Yang immediately burst out laughing, "Hahaha, how did you go bald? Have you really become a monk?"

Lu Yang tried to touch Old Meng’s head but was impatiently slapped away by Meng Jingzhou, "Scram, scram, scram."

"Wasn’t it because I received a mission? They said someone’s daughter had gone missing in Buddha Country. I followed the clues here to search for her and had to infiltrate a temple, so I had no choice but to shave my head."

"Did you find the person who went missing?"

"Found her. She hadn’t gone missing at all; she had eloped with a member of the Demon Race. I followed the trail they left all the way to the vicinity of Western Heaven City, and that’s where I found them. I told them to come back with me to Great Xia and get married properly; no harm done. But they wouldn’t listen and even claimed their love was free."

"I couldn’t be bothered to explain, so I just took the daughter. That Demon Race youngster had some cultivation level and, his eyes red with rage, insisted on having a go at me. As if his little cultivation level could beat me! I slapped the lad and sent him flying."

"After delivering the daughter to her father, I swung by the Western Paradise Temple to try out their mutton hotpot, and there I bumped into you."

Lu Yang flicked his finger, using the Eternity Technique to help Meng Jingzhou grow his hair back, and soon Meng Jingzhou once again had a head full of thick hair.

Meng Jingzhou happily stroked his hair, "Your cultivation level has really improved, eh? You can use the Eternity Technique without even running into me."

"Not bad, I guess. I’ve had some insights in my recent cultivation and made some progress. It’s not much but definitely better than you."

"Oh?" A strong combat spirit flashed in Meng Jingzhou’s eyes, "Getting cocky after becoming a cook, are you?"

Lu Yang still had that smile, "I can fight you with one hand tied behind my back."

"I don’t need your charity; give it all you’ve got!"

Meng Jingzhou bellowed, activating the Supreme Pure Yang Dharma Image, a hundred-foot-tall Dharma Aspect wielding spear and shield, awe-inspiring.

Then Meng Jingzhou saw Lu Yang use Law of Heaven and Earth, transforming into a giant tens of thousands of feet tall, and stepping over with one foot, which was even larger than his own Dharma Aspect.

Meng Jingzhou fiercely remembered the things Lu Yang had bragged about.

"Old Lu, you damn became an Immortal in Buddha Country, shameless!"

Lu Yang’s thunderous, dull voice came from above Meng Jingzhou’s head:

"If you can’t win, admit it. No excuses."

With one foot stomping down, Meng Jingzhou was squashed back to his original form.

Meng Jingzhou climbed out of the sand pit, dirty and disgruntled, cursing at Lu Yang, "Lu Yang, you son of a..."

A stunningly beautiful woman in a sky-blue dress flew out of Lu Yang’s body, stopping Meng Jingzhou’s outburst, "Don’t use foul language."

The elders are still watching in the Spiritual Space; even scolding Lu Yang shouldn’t be in front of the elders; it would dirty their ears.

After saying that, Qinghe returned to the Spiritual Space, leaving Meng Jingzhou dumbfounded.

"Did you swap out someone in your Spiritual Space?"

Lu Yang sighed, "No, just added one more person."

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes widened. How popular was this kid Lu Yang’s Spiritual Space that not only had he gained a new tenant, but the tenant was such a peerless beauty?

The two left Buddha Country and returned to the Seek Dao Sect. Just as they entered the Sect, they saw Yun Mengmeng, Ao Ling, Jiang Lianyi, and Jin Caiwei welcoming Lu Yang back.

Meng Jingzhou: "..."

Chapter 1116: Chapter 115 Intrigues

"Second-in-command, I’ve found another delicious treat, want to try?" Yun Mengmeng carried a bamboo basket, which was covered with a layer of cloth, hiding whatever treat was inside.

"Elder Brother Lu Yang, you interact with Immortal Sister more often. Does Immortal Sister mention me or Lianyi more?" Ao Ling stood to Lu Yang’s left, her tone gentle yet firm.

"Since Immortal Sister and I are so close, of course she mentions me more!" Jiang Lianyi stood to Lu Yang’s right, glaring at Ao Ling.

"Young Sect Master, do you think there is any room for improvement in the Recording Orb?" Jin Caiwei held up the Recording Orb, trying hard to sway it in front of Lu Yang.

The four ladies surrounded Lu Yang, each with their requests, overwhelming him completely.

Meng Jingzhou raised his hand, wanting to use the Single Curse Fist, but he paused, clueless about whom he could hit since he couldn’t beat any of them.

He took an Oblivion Pill, and instantly his mind was as calm as still water. Then he saw Lu Yang surrounded by the four women, felt jealousy surge again, took another Oblivion Pill, and the jealousy returned.

Meng Jingzhou took a deep breath and decided not to look at the scene that filled him with jealousy, resolutely turning to head to the Task Hall.

Lu Yang noticed Meng Jingzhou’s unusual behavior and shouted, "Hey Old Meng, why are you leaving? You haven’t finished telling us about your experiences in the Buddha Country!"

"I’m not telling it anymore. Your experiences are far more exciting!"

Lu Yang was confused. Why had Old Meng suddenly become upset? Had he overdone it with his guidance using his Immortal Body?

That shouldn’t be the case, he had only offered a foot of guidance. Old Meng wasn’t that fragile, right?

"Second-in-command, taste this, taste this."

"...Sister Mengmeng, I’ll eat, I’ll eat, just don’t poke my face with the food."

Lu Yang, overwhelmed, ate it in one bite, not knowing what it was, but indeed, it tasted very good.

Yun Mengmeng, hearing Lu Yang praising her homemade pastry as delicious, became even more excited: "Try another piece; it tastes different."

Lu Yang was surrounded by the four women all the way from the entrance of the Seek Dao Sect back to Sky Gate Mountain.

At each side of Lu Yang were the ancestors of Dragon and Phoenix. He didn’t know what had happened during the time he walked, but the conflict between these two seemed to have intensified.

Both ancestors looked eagerly at Lu Yang, hoping to hear the answers they wanted to hear.

Lu Yang showed a troubled expression: "Elder Ao Ling, Elder Lianyi, this question is hard to answer."

"His Majesty brings you up every day; the count is beyond my ability to tally. How can I possibly rank you?"

Hearing Lu Yang say this, both women looked challengingly at each other, dispelling much of the tension-filled atmosphere, yet deep down, they were very pleased.

Lu Yang felt ashamed for not being able to provide a clear answer to the two women and quickly tried to rectify: "If you really want to know the answer, it’s simple. Senior Qinghe is now the Historian; she can help keep count in the future."

Senior Qinghe, who was currently in the Spiritual Space feeding Immortal Fairy, stiffened. How did this problem end up being tossed to her?

She covered the Immortal Fairy with a small blanket, her voice gentle: "Milord, I will be away for a moment."

The Immortal Fairy lay in bed, still appearing frail, and hummed lightly, feeling that the outside was very lively and wishing it was nice.

Qinghe flew out of the Spiritual Space, glaring at Lu Yang, suspecting he did it on purpose.

"Sister Qinghe, from now on, we’ll rely on you to keep count."

"The tasks assigned by the two sisters are certainly within Qinghe’s duties. Every word and action of His Majesty carries profound meanings."

"Perhaps there’s no answer to the two sisters’ problem," he said.

"What do you mean?"

Faced with Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi, Qinghe adopted a severely troubled expression, "These past few days, while serving as Historian and taking care of His Majesty, I’ve noticed some differences from Ancient Times. Previously, His Majesty often mentioned the two of you, but now he mostly speaks of Lu Yang."

Lu Yang subtly took over the conversation from Qinghe, "Senior Qinghe is right. His Majesty often tells me that our Great Bean Dynasty is full of talented individuals. If we could abandon internal strife, cooperate with each other, and work together, there is nothing in this world we cannot overcome."

Lu Yang glared at Qinghe. Listen, what does it mean to take care of a Fairy as a Historian? Is that really a Historian’s job?

Qinghe glared back at Lu Yang. What kind of enchantment have you fed to His Majesty, with him talking only about you!

Lu Yang felt that he and Qinghe wouldn’t be able to determine the winner anytime soon, so he quickly changed the topic and thought of a new way for the Qiongqi Clan to get rich.

"Senior Caiwei, there is indeed room for improvement with the Recording Orb. I was supposed to discuss this with you earlier, but I got delayed by some matters. Please, come with me."

Jin Caiwei’s eyes lit up, knowing that the Young Sect Master still had solutions, and hurriedly followed him.

...

Tao Yaoye was lying at the entrance of her abode on a peach tree, holding a branch and lost in thought. Perceiving Lu Yang’s arrival, she immediately jumped down, straightened her clothes, and waved towards Lu Yang.

"Elder Brother Lu Yang, I heard you’ve returned from Demon City..."

Then she saw a group of beautiful women behind Lu Yang and was immediately stunned, her hand frozen in the air before she remembered to put it down.

"Sister Mengmeng, I’m here." Yun Mengmeng saw Tao Yaoye waving and imitated her.

She had lived in the Seek Dao Sect for so long and was very familiar with Tao Yaoye.

Lu Yang coughed and said, "Ahem, Junior Sister Tao, let me introduce them. These are Senior Ao Ling, Senior Jiang Lianyi, Senior Jin Caiwei, and Senior Qinghe."

As a member of the Heavenly Court Sect, Tao Yaoye was aware of the existence of Ao Ling and the others, but it was the first time she was meeting them formally like today.

Tao Yaoye hurriedly paid her respects, "Tao Yaoye greets the seniors!"

At the same time, she felt relieved. Since they were all seniors, they probably wouldn’t become her romantic rivals, and her advantage was still considerable.

Her biggest enemy now was Yun Mengmeng. This Yun Mengmeng, harder to handle than Lan Ting, was meticulous in her thoughts. Tao Yaoye repeatedly probed indirectly but was cleverly evaded by her opponent, unable to discern Yun Mengmeng’s true intentions!

"Senior Caiwei, this is the method I was speaking of."

Lu Yang continued with a smile, "You might have heard of my Junior Sister Tao, the founder of Dream Mirage."

Jin Caiwei certainly had heard. Tao Yaoye, despite her initial low cultivation level, had created Dream Mirage, which must have accumulated to a tremendous extent by now.

"I was thinking the Senior could try integrating the Recording Orb with Dream Mirage, using the Recording Orb to display the content of Dream Mirage. This could significantly boost the sales of the Recording Orb."

"However, Senior would need to periodically share the profits with my Junior Sister. How does that sound to you?"

"No problem!" Although Jin Caiwei lacked a business mind, she trusted in Lu Yang’s wisdom.

"Junior Sister Tao, what do you think?"

Tao Yaoye saw the benefits of the move, which would expand Dream Mirage’s channels and also foster a good relationship with Senior Caiwei.

Apart from Elder Brother Lu Yang’s mediation, this was akin to relying on her own merits to establish a profit-sharing partnership with an Ancient Half-Immortal—an opportunity many cultivators could not even dream of.

Although she hadn’t seen Elder Brother Lu Yang for some time, Elder Brother Lu Yang was indeed still thinking of her!

Chapter 1117: Chapter 1116: The Second Strongest in Seek Dao Sect

Somewhere in the Seek Dao Sect, three Daoist figures gathered rarely and had a brief drink together.

"Come, a toast to the Seek Dao Sect!" Celestial Master Guiyuan raised his glass and said.

"A toast."

"Cheers!"

Daoist Xiantian and Vast Sea Daoist Lord clinked their glasses together.

Since his emergence, Celestial Master Guiyuan spent his days visiting friends, going from Five Elements Sect to the Suspension Temple, and from there to the Imperial City. After battles, he would chat and boast with friends, living leisurely and carefree.

Especially when he heard his friends praising the talent of Yun Zhi from his sect, they all expressed envy, which pleased Celestial Master Guiyuan greatly.

Upon his return in high spirits, he invited the other two ancestors for a gathering and even brought out Spirit Wine that had been sealed for a hundred thousand years.

"Ancestor, I toast to you," Vast Sea Daoist Lord raised his glass to Celestial Master Guiyuan.

"Ancestor, I toast to you," Celestial Master Guiyuan toasted Daoist Xiantian.

"Master, I toast to you," Daoist Xiantian toasted Vast Sea Daoist Lord.

The gathering of the three ancestors of Seek Dao Sect was indeed a fortunate and fulfilling event.

"It’s embarrassing to think that the Seek Dao Sect I founded has achieved such success. Sadly, I am now the one with the lowest cultivation level here," Daoist Xiantian said self-deprecatingly, feeling somewhat down.

"What are you talking about, Grand Master? The Seek Dao Sect you founded during the Great Yu Era was a rare and righteous sect, known for promoting justice and vanquishing evil, praised by all," Celestial Master Guiyuan genuinely admired Daoist Xiantian, able to stay untainted amidst chaos in the Great Yu Era was indeed rare.

"Indeed, it is because you led us that our Seek Dao Sect has always upheld the righteous path and left behind a good reputation. Now everyone praises our sect as the foremost sect of the righteous path!"

Hearing this from Celestial Master Guiyuan, Daoist Xiantian’s mood improved significantly, "A toast."

"I can’t believe that during the time I was confined, our sect saw the rise of Xiao Yun, such a genius that I’ve been pushed to second place in terms of strength within the Seek Dao Sect," Celestial Master Guiyuan exclaimed with emotion.

He had sparred with Vast Sea Daoist Lord and had a slight edge over him.

"Grand Master, you might not necessarily be the second strongest in our sect," Vast Sea Daoist Lord cautioned.

"You may not be aware, but our sect has two guest elders who are actually the second strongest."

Celestial Master Guiyuan was greatly surprised, "Our sect has guest elders? Who are they?"

"They are the Dragon Clan Ancestor Ao Ling and Phoenix Ancestor Jiang Lianyi."

"It turns out to be them," Celestial Master Guiyuan got serious, not expecting these formidable figures to be guest elders in the sect.

Celestial Master Guiyuan suddenly became enthusiastic; he loved to challenge the strong, especially figures from ancient times such as these.

"Where are they now? I want to train with them."

Just the right moment to see who truly is the second strongest in Seek Dao Sect!

...

"From what Celestial Master Guiyuan implies, does he want to test the skills of the two of us?" Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi also became interested; they were quite curious about Celestial Master Guiyuan’s Guiyi Tao Fruit Outline.

And as for the title of the second strongest of the Seek Dao Sect, they were interested in it as well.

Moreover, they were also generals of the Great Bean Dynasty, with the Immortal Sister watching over Elder Brother Lu Yang’s spiritual space, they could not possibly refuse a challenge.

"Second-in-command, is this going to turn into a fight? Should we try to intervene?" Yun Mengmeng whispered.

"Let’s not interfere, just watch," Lu Yang whispered back,—these were elders, and they could not be persuaded.

"Shall we pick a spot?"

Celestial Master Guiyuan led everyone to a deep part of the sect, the area was vast, big enough for their fight.

"Second-in-command, this spot here," Yun Mengmeng picked an excellent spot for watching, calling over Lu Yang to spread out a blanket and a dazzling array of food. fгeewebnovёl.com

Daoist Xiantian, never having seen so much delicious food before, nearly drooled.

Jin Caiwei felt that life in the Seek Dao Sect was truly wonderful, not only were food and drink abundant, but watching semi-immortal battles frequently also accumulated experience, much better than staying with their Qiongqi Clan.

Not far away, the peaks of two mountains emitted an aura that forbade strangers, hosting the battle of the Seek Dao Sect’s four unparalleled experts. Had the outside world known of this battle, it would undoubtedly have caused a huge uproar.

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi transformed in an instant, becoming a towering black dragon and a golden phoenix. Together, they roared, and the heavens and earth trembled!

"Truly, an Ancient Demon!" Celestial Master Guiyuan said with a solemn expression, facing such formidable foes with no room for carelessness.

"Indeed," the Vast Sea Daoist Lord said, simply standing nearby and feeling the profound aura of historical weight emanating from the Dragon and Phoenix Ancestors.

Truly, they were beings on the brink of attaining immortality!

Ao Ling made the first move, stretching out his dragon claw and shattering the space, which instantly burst apart; he used brute force to employ the "Shrinking Ground Into Inches," shortening the distance between him and Celestial Master Guiyuan and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord.

Ao Ling moved so swiftly that even a seasoned Semi-Immortal like Celestial Master Guiyuan couldn’t react in time.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord activated his Embryonic Spatial Dao Fruit, instantly stretching the distance between him and Ao Ling to an infinite extent, rendering Ao Ling’s "Earth Shrinking" useless.

Celestial Master Guiyuan deployed the "Palm Thunder," using the Guiyi Tao Fruit outline to merge himself and the Palm Thunder into one entity, transforming into an invisible yet untouchable Thunder Spirit!

Yingtian Immortal had once used this technique; Jiang Lianyi handled it with ease, instantly transforming into a fire phoenix that sparked Nirvana True Fire everywhere it passed. Whole mountains were set ablaze by the Nirvana True Fire, filling the region with dense Yang Qi, comparable to the surface of the sun!

When Thunder Spirit collided with the Fire Phoenix, they whipped up a storm of thunder and flames. Even sitting at a great distance, Lu Yang felt a tingling sensation on his skin—a result of the clash between thunder and fire, filling this space with their energies.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord leapt through space, avoiding direct contact with Ao Ling and instead attempting a sneak attack to gradually weaken Ao Ling’s aura.

However, Ao Ling’s aura didn’t decrease but instead surged. His physical strength quietly escalated until the Vast Sea Daoist Lord realized his strike couldn’t even scrape off Ao Ling’s dragon scales!

Her physical strength had reached the level of an Immortal Body!

Ao Ling extended his dragon claw—his formidable physical strength allowing him to completely disregard the Embryonic Spatial Dao Fruit, crossing the space and leaving three claw marks across the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s chest!

"Innate Ren Water!"

Every drop of water beneath Ao Ling’s feet could transform into vast lakes, created from the mingling of the three types of Innate Divine Waters from the sun, moon, and stars, forming oceans that roared toward the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, washing him up against the opposite mountain peak!

"Vast Sea!"

For a moment, Celestial Master Guiyuan and Jiang Lianyi were evenly matched and, noticing the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s early defeat, hurried to his aid.

If the Vast Sea Daoist Lord were utterly out of the fight, then facing a two-against-one battle, he surely couldn’t win!

Cradling his chest, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord grimaced, "It’s nothing major; it’s just that this Immortal Body is really hard to deal with."

Celestial Master Guiyuan, having clashed with Meng Junzi, knew the formidable nature of the Immortal Body.

"Should we use that move?"

"Let’s go!"

The two exchanged a glance and decided to use their ultimate technique to counteract the Dragon and Phoenix Ancestors.

"Guiyi!"

Their forms gradually turned ethereal, merging into a new entity.

Ao Ling, who had been ready to pursue her advantage, abruptly halted. She sensed a threat emanating from them, one that was capable of threatening an Immortal Body!

"A Unification technique, huh? That’s indeed rare," Jiang Lianyi remarked, recognizing the difficulty of this move.

"But it’s not enough to defeat us. We have a Unification technique too!"

The Dragon and Phoenix Ancestors circled in the sky, portecken surrounding their omen, the heavens trembling!

The will to battle was intense on both sides, each with reasons they couldn’t afford to lose!

"Second-in-command, who do you think will win?" Yun Mengmeng asked while munching on a cookie, her words muffled.

Lu Yang wore a strange expression, "It’s hard to say who will win, but I remember they are vying to be the second strongest in the Seek Dao Sect, right?"

"That’s right."

"Isn’t the second strongest supposed to be a fairy?"

"Then they are competing for the third strongest?"

"But the third strongest is Guan Shanhai."

Chapter 1118: Chapter 117 Little Lu, this position of Sect Leader is destined to be yours!

Dragon and Phoenix intertwined, their momentum grew increasingly strong, the heavens and earth mourned with deafening roars, causing both the Unification of Celestial Master Guiyuan and Vast Sea Daoist Lord to change their expressions.

This was a move that had never appeared in any ancient text nor had it ever been displayed in public before.

Dragon Phoenix Transformation!

Unlike the book written by Daoist Buyu, this was the real "Dragon Phoenix Transformation."

Although Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi often quarreled, they were truly close sisters. Together, they had finally developed this terrifying unification technique.

To be honest, Lu Yang really couldn’t understand why the two sides needed to fight at all. Was it necessary to mobilize such forces just for the position of the fourth strongest in the Seek Dao Sect?

Although Guan Shanhai was imprisoned at Captive Peak, after all, Captive Peak was still within Seek Dao Sect’s territory, and the prisoners belonged to Seek Dao Sect.

Of course, after being released from prison, they would belong to whichever force they belonged to.

As for the fourth strongest, it wasn’t easy to rank. There weren’t few Semi-Immortals in the Seek Dao Sect, not to mention in Captive Peak alone; both the Void Venerate and the Nightmare Supreme were entities that could potentially establish dynasties.

If they didn’t fight, it really wouldn’t be clear who was the fourth strongest.

"Isn’t the fourth you, Second-in-command?" Yun Mengmeng asked puzzledly; the Second-in-command possessed an Immortal Body, even able to kill an avatar of the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, definitely a contender for the fourth strongest in the Seek Dao Sect.

"Eh, eh, eh, you can’t just say that," Lu Yang jumped in shock. How could he, with his merits and capabilities, be the fourth strongest of the Seek Dao Sect? What would happen if this rumor spread?

Originally brimming with the intent to fight and cause heaven and earth flipping, the four combatants lost all will to fight upon hearing Lu Yang speak.

"Shall we not fight then?"

Ao Ling took the initiative, feeling that fighting so fiercely just to compete for the fourth spot in the Seek Dao Sect wasn’t worth it.

Both the Unification of Celestial Master Guiyuan and Vast Sea Daoist Lord nodded at the same time; there was no point in fighting over the fourth rank.

It was just unknown who the "Fairy" Lu Yang mentioned was.

The firebird extinguished, Immortal Body retracted, and unification dissolved.

"Hmm, why aren’t we fighting anymore?" Lu Yang was pondering who could really be the fourth strongest, suddenly realizing it had gone silent around him.

He looked up to find the four who were just fighting all gathered around him.

Lu Yang got another big shock, fearing they wanted to challenge him for the fourth rank of the Seek Dao Sect.

"Little Lu, who is this ’Fairy’ you just mentioned?" Celestial Master Guiyuan was particularly curious; this "Fairy" was ranked ahead of the Great Yu National Preceptor Guan Shanhai—who could this distinguished person be?

Lu Yang was startled; he had just been quietly chatting with Yun Mengmeng; could his soft voice really have been overheard?

"Uh..." Lu Yang stammered, uncertain whether he should reveal the existence of the Fairy.

At that moment, from the Spiritual Space came the voice of the Fairy, "It’s okay, Little Yang. My existence is hardly a secret."

An enchanting silhouette drifted out from Lu Yang’s body, her beauty breathtakingly peerless, causing anyone to sincerely admire her stunning appearance.

The face of Fairy Eternity was cool as ice, her brows exuded an unquestionable authority, instilling involuntary respect in others, her bright yellow dress emanating an indescribable sense of opulence.

"Immortal?!"

Both Celestial Master Guiyuan and Vast Sea Daoist Lord were shocked at once; this aura was clearly that of an Immortal!

So Lu Yang had an Immortal within him?

"May I know you are..."

"I am the leader of the Five Ancient Immortals, Immortal Fairy Eternity, and also one of the Guest Elders of the Seek Dao Sect." When introducing herself, Fairy Eternity’s tone was cold, as if she was a great existence that had transcended ages and witnessed the rise and fall of many.

Lu Yang looked up in surprise at Immortal Fairy Eternity. Fairy, have you changed your personality?

Celestial Master Guiyuan and Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s pupils shrank suddenly, "The chief of the Five Ancient Immortals, what an incredibly prestigious title!"

But weren’t there only four immortals in ancient times? Wait, could this be the person who confronted the Four Ancient Immortals and forced them to reshape the continent?

Thinking of this, both of them became even more respectful.

"In that recent battle in the Demon Territory..."

"It was also my doing."

The two sucked in a breath of cold air, completely shocked, a word that barely described their emotions.

They also envied Lu Yang’s fortune, for the leader of the Five Ancient Immortals to reside in his Spiritual Space was a heaven-sent opportunity.

Possibly no one from the past till now had ever possessed such a fortune.

"Thou shalt not speak of my presence."

"Yes!"

Before the two could say anything else, Immortal Fairy turned into a wisp of blue smoke and floated back to the Spiritual Space, eagerly asking Qinghe.

"How was it, was my performance satisfactory just now?"

"My lord’s presence spans eternity, and his grace is as the rain and thunder from the heavens, truly admirable."

"That’s good."

Immortal Fairy thought contentedly, it seems the teachings of the Yingtian Immortal Sect still work.

Her appearance this time was not just about herself; it also represented Little Yang’s face, so she couldn’t afford to be as casual as before.

Daoist Xiantian looked at Lu Yang very excitedly, his eyes even filled with some adoration.

When the Third Ancestor of Seek Dao Sect learned of Immortal Fairy’s existence, he was both shocked and pleased, that even the chief of the Five Ancient Immortals was their guest elder. He looked at Lu Yang with increasing favor.

Presumably, that being was willing to become a guest elder also in consideration of Lu Yang.

"Little Lu, do well, and the position of Sect Leader shall undoubtedly be yours!" Celestial Master Guiyuan urged, patting Lu Yang’s shoulders vigorously. In his time, the position of Sect Leader was highly sought after.

Anyone who said Lu Yang couldn’t be the Sect Leader, he would be furious at them.

Since there was no need for battle, the Third Ancestor of Seek Dao didn’t stay and continued back to his drinking.

Lu Yang recalled the days when Immortal Fairy acted as the Sect Leader, feeling the future might not be that promising.

"Little Yang, don’t worry, if Miss Yun doesn’t let you be the Sect Leader, then the two of us will join forces and defeat her!" Immortal Fairy declared she would always be Lu Yang’s solid support.

Lu Yang felt this support wasn’t very solid either.

The first round was the Qian Heaven Thunder Tribulation; what would follow could only be some kind of demons or monsters!

"Heavenly Reversal!"

When Lu Yang was passing his Nascent Soul Perfection tribulation, he had relied on this trick to fool the Qian Heaven Thunder Tribulation, hoping to repeat the trick.

But whether he became Lu Yin or remained Lu Yang, the thunder tribulation struck unerringly, impossible to deceive!

Lu Yang realized that last time he had succeeded because the thunder tribulation was uncontrolled; this time, with the Yingtian Immortal watching, fooling it would be preposterous!

The ruthless purple glow thrashed them, bathing them in the thunder tribulation. They were slashed open, skin flayed, and one could smell the charred scent of their singed hair and blackened bodies resembling lumps of charcoal.

"We finally got through it." Meng Jingzhou spoke, exhaling black smoke, his voice hoarse, still terrified, thinking he was about to die.

Fortunately, they had made it through; their physical bodies were extraordinary, and despite being mutilated, they were still automatically recovering their strength and physique.

However, before they could even grasp the situation, the second round of the thunder tribulation followed, giving them no chance to catch their breath!

"It’s coming again?!" Both men looked shocked, abandoning all pretense and greedily gulping down elixirs to restore their condition.

A thunder tribulation of myriad colors descended, like someone had kicked over a bucket of paint, turning the colors of the lightning bizarre and wondrous, omnipotent, annihilating everything.

"How do I feel this thunder tribulation is even more terrifying than the Qian Heaven Thunder Tribulation?" A newly admitted disciple, although unfamiliar with the classifications of thunder tribulations, was unusually sensitive to danger.

Dai Bufan had a strange expression, racking his brains but unable to match any known thunder tribulations with this second round: "I’ve never seen this kind of thunder tribulation. Could there be new types cropping up even after three hundred thousand years?"

"And its power is clearly stronger than that of the Qian Heaven Thunder Tribulation. Has the Qian Heaven Thunder Tribulation evolved to be the second thunder tribulation for the Divinity Transformation Stage?"

Why does everything involving Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou always turn out so odd?

Looking at them attempting to pass the tribulation was like witnessing history.

The lightning was splendid, shaking heaven and earth; the sky was painted in dazzling, variegated colors as if a great catastrophe was descending.

Suddenly, silence fell, the thunder tribulation still present but no longer making any sound.

Great sound is often silent!

The quiet lasted only a moment before the world’s sounds returned, and the thunder tribulation surged even more fiercely, fiercely raining down on Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

Lu Yang wielded his sword, Meng Jingzhou his fist, attempting to destroy the thunder tribulation before it could fully descend.

Unfortunately, against the thunder tribulation meticulously prepared for them by the Yingtian Immortal, all resistance was futile.

The thunder tribulation pierced through Lu Yang along the Green Peak Sword, and simultaneously, a fist seal struck Meng Jingzhou.

After the second round of the thunder tribulation, both men felt their marrow and blood imbued with electricity. They were in such a sorry state that it was difficult to even discern their identities, let alone distinguish whether they were male or female by outsiders.

Faced with the imminent and unknown third round of thunder tribulation, which intuitively seemed even more terrifying than the second, they knew it absolutely must not descend!

Meng Jingzhou seemed to recall something and hurriedly shouted to the heavens to clarify his position:

"We’re your own people, ah! I can recite the ’Immortal’s Quotations’ backwards!"

The impending third round of thunder tribulation suddenly froze; just when Meng Jingzhou thought he had succeeded, he saw the thunder tribulation transform again, becoming even denser based on what had occurred before, as if someone had increased its power at the last moment, making it feel even more dangerous.

The dense, almost white thunder tribulation descended, reflecting the despair on their faces.

Chapter 1123: Chapter 1122: My Fate Is In My Own Hands, Not Dictated By Heaven!

Lu Yang’s face was scorched black, and upon hearing Meng Jingzhou shout about being able to recite the Immortal’s Quotations backwards, he instantly turned pale as a ghost.

This intensified third round of Thunder Tribulation looked like it was set to annihilate someone.

He had originally intended to set Old Meng up, but instead, he had trapped himself miserably.

"Damn it, Old Lu, you set me up!" Recalling the peculiarities of the third round of Thunder Tribulation, Meng Jingzhou instantly realized he had been played.

So much for the Yingtian Immortal Device favoring Old Lu—it was clearly Old Lu who had somehow provoked the Yingtian Immortal, resulting in himself getting dragged into the mess!

And the likely reason was probably found in this "Immortal’s Quotations"!

"Ah?"

The Meng Family was the most prominent influential family and also a family of officials. Meng Jingzhou, well-versed in the intrigues of government, was at a loss trying to connect ’Historian’ with ’autocratic rule’.

Old Lu’s antics with the Immortal seemed quite varied.

In an instant, Lu Yang’s body was enveloped in Sword Qi, bravely confronting the Thunder Tribulation. The pure and spotless white Thunder Tribulation struck Lu Yang, allowing Meng Jingzhou, who stood beside him, to see Lu Yang’s bones.

Yingtian Immortal, floating in the sky, watched Lu Yang with confusion, not understanding what the youngster was attempting to do.

Even though Lu Yang had successfully shattered a strand of Thunder Tribulation, more thunder followed one after another, leaving Lu Yang overwhelmed.

And Elder Brother Dai, what are you so excited about? You’re shouting the loudest!

He always enjoyed striking at those who declared their fate was in their own hands, not in heaven’s. Did they really think his Thunder Tribulation was vegetarian?

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were evenly matched in their struggle against the Thunder Tribulation, but just as they reached a delicate balance, the power of the thunder increased once more. Both were struck so hard by the Thunder Tribulation that they wished for death. Lu Yang was hit back to his original form, with the nine Immortal Swords scattered around him.

The two fell head-first into the ground, looking like newly planted saplings, twitching from the lightning strikes.

Using their palms to prop themselves up, they burst from the ground and lay there, watching the final Thunder Tribulation brewing in the sky, the corners of their eyes twitching.

Chapter 1124: Chapter 1123: Void Refinement Stage

"No, no, no, I don’t want to listen!" Having been deceived by Lu Yang once, Meng Jingzhou was not about to be fooled again. Seeing that Lu Yang still wanted to speak, he immediately covered his mouth.

Seeing that Old Meng was not fooled, Lu Yang had no choice but to prepare for the final Thunder Tribulation.

"Although it’s still theoretical, the opportunity is rare, so it’s worth a try."

Lu Yang lay on the ground, becoming one with the earth, planting the Bodhi Seed. In an instant, the Bodhi Tree blossomed and bore fruit, giving birth to Lu Yang and his Wooden Avatar.

His primordial spirit left his body and merged into the Wooden Avatar. The Wooden Avatar exhibited Imitation Fist and transformed into the shape of the Green Peak Sword. Then, executing Ten Thousand Swords Returning to Origin, the Wooden Avatar and nine swords unified, held by Lu Yang.

"I always feel your moves are several times more complicated than others."

"You’re the one who talks too much. Today, you’ll witness the true power of the Immortal Sword Technique!"

Wielding the Self Sword, Lu Yang confronted the Heavenly Tribulation alone, a scene of tragic heroism.

Lu Yang swung the Immortal Sword, his posture graceful, resembling a transcended Sword Immortal. Every movement carried a unique rhythm. If any Sword Cultivator were present, their understanding of Swordsmanship would have undoubtedly ascended.

The only downside was that Lu Yang’s body was charred black as if he had crawled out of a coal pile.

"Hm?" Meng Jingzhou noticed the change in Lu Yang, surprised, and no longer lay on the ground playing dead. He stood up to see what Lu Yang intended to do.

He sensed that Lu Yang’s sword moved with his heart, achieving Unity of Essence, Qi, and Spirit. This wasn’t surprising, as Lu Yang’s sword was inherently a part of him.

However, he then sensed that Lu Yang’s strength was concentrated in his right arm, which showed signs of being unable to bear his body’s power, his fine blood vessels bursting directly.

Crack—

The final bolt of Heavenly Lightning descended, vast across the sky, plummeting down, but Lu Yang faced it head-on.

"Slash!"

The Self Sword unleashed a dazzling sword light, the strongest Lu Yang had ever produced, so overpowering that even Body Integration Realm Sword Cultivators felt inferior.

Lu Yang, who thrived in battle, found both pressure and motivation in the Heavenly Lightning, helping him complete the last piece of the Immortal Sword Technique.

The sword light split the Heavenly Lightning, seemingly cleaving it in two!

Boom—

To execute this strike, Lu Yang poured all his energy into it, pushing his right arm to the limit of its endurance until it exploded!

Meng Jingzhou was shocked. Was Lu Yang practicing a self-harming sword technique? His arm exploded; it was practically self-detonation, which they wouldn’t expect to recover from quickly even at the Body Integration Realm!

Unexpectedly, Lu Yang released the Self Sword and transformed into a spiritual energy life-form, consuming spiritual energy to compensate for the deficiency. When he regained human form, his right arm was restored to its original state, leaving Meng Jingzhou’s eyes nearly popping out.

"How is that possible?!"

Lu Yang twisted his arm, feeling no discomfort. Indeed, his approach was correct.

The lightning split into two, striking both Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

Finally drained of strength, both collapsed to the ground with a thud.

As the Heavenly Tribulation ended, nectar descended, nourishing their bodies. They floated in the air, their wounds silently healing.

Both officially entered the Void Refinement Stage!

"Finally reached the Void Refinement... How did we get back to the Qi Cultivation Stage?"

Both were astonished by the sudden drop to the lowest realm, their powers returning to the initial state of cultivation, now unable to defeat even a Tiger Demon.

In the Void Refinement Stage, there was erratic leaping from the Qi Cultivation Stage to the Body Integration Realm without any pattern. Cultivators in this realm seldom left their homes to avoid being killed by Foundation Establishment Great Masters.

Although they had learned about the unique manifestations of the Void Refinement Stage beforehand, accepting them still wasn’t easy once they reached this realm.

"Now we’re back in the Nascent Soul Stage."

In an instant, they both leaped to the Nascent Soul Stage, the changes rapid. The swift shifts in realm meant they couldn’t even control their own strength properly—one second they used the strength of the Qi Cultivation Stage to walk, the next they were in the Nascent Soul Stage, potentially covering hundreds of feet in a single step.

"Strange, where did these petals come from?"

Daoist Xiantian was puzzled when suddenly petals drifted above his head.

Everyone looked up to see that after passing the Tribulation, the thunderclouds had not dissipated but instead had split open to reveal sunshine and a flurry of petals. From within the sunlight, the emperor-like, slender figure emerged, overlooking the mortals.

He had seen countless trials; his eyes held the vicissitudes of life. Nothing that appeared before him could sway his decision; he fulfilled all mortal fantasies about immortals.

The emperor-like figure appeared silhouetted against the light, his face indiscernible, signifying that mortals should not gaze upon the countenance of an immortal.

When he spoke, the world hushed, as if his was the only voice in existence, and even the sounds of insects and birds completely vanished.

"Heh, who would have thought that such extraordinary talents would appear in later generations."

The members of the Seek Dao Sect were thrown into chaos, unable to believe that additional changes could occur during a Heavenly Tribulation, something unprecedented from ancient times to the present.
